Chinese Eastern Railway Dispute

Russian General Representative

Insists on Not Returning Locomotives

Japanese Official Circles Indicate Unwillingness to Purchase

Rumors of Russian Troops Digging Trenches on the Border

Workers on Eastern Section of Railway Go on Strike

Retired Employees Demand Back Pay

(Harbin) Although the railway dispute between "Manchukuo" and Soviet Russia has led to an exchange of diplomatic notes between the "Manchukuo" government and the Soviet Russian General Representative of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Kushniakov, for diplomatic negotiations, the situation remains tense. It is rumored that about a thousand Russian soldiers have dug trenches within Manzhouli and are stationed on the border to prevent incidents. The Russian soldiers are now drilling daily and can be seen in Manzhouli, causing great panic among the residents on the border. It is reported that the Russian soldiers have fourteen pursuit guns and a large number of machine guns. Workers at some stations on the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway, such as Yimianpo, are currently on strike, reportedly due to Communist propaganda. Traffic has not been severely affected. It is rumored that the Russian General Manager of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Rudy, has moved to the Soviet Russian Consulate, indicating that someone intends to harm him. Currently, both sides are reviewing documents related to the Chinese Eastern Railway. It is reported that the Russian General Representative insists that "Manchukuo" has certain rights to freight cars, but about six hundred have already been returned. As for the locomotives, they belong to Soviet Russia and therefore cannot be returned according to "Manchukuo's" request. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

(Harbin) Retired employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway recently held a meeting here and found that about 700 people are living in extreme poverty because the railway authorities have refused to pay their arrears. It is claimed that the railway authorities still owe these retired employees 1.5 million gold rubles. The meeting decided to send representatives of the retired employees to demand that the railway authorities pay all the arrears in the first half of the year. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Official circles criticized Soviet Russia's letter regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway, stating that Japan is prepared to pay for the transportation of Japanese troops on the Chinese Eastern Railway, but requests that the fees be reduced according to the reduced fees previously charged for transporting Chinese troops on the railway. Japan has already deposited the amount due according to this method into the Chinese Eastern Railway account. As for the locomotives and freight cars detained by Soviet Russia, Soviet Russia should return them because the Chinese Eastern Railway is a joint Russian-Manchu enterprise according to the 1924 treaty. Japan has no intention of buying the Chinese Eastern Railway. Due to the completion of competing routes, its economic value has greatly diminished. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

Finance Minister Song Arrives in Kobe to Attend Washington Conference

Deeply Concerned About Raising the Sino-Japanese Issue

Japanese Government Discusses Countermeasures

Kobe The Jefferson General, the ship carrying Song Ziwen, arrived here at noon today. Song stayed in his cabin and refused to meet with the large number of Japanese reporters who boarded the ship. Song issued a brief statement through the Chinese Consul General stationed here, saying that the situation is critical and it is not convenient to discuss anything. After arriving in Seattle, Song and his advisors and secretaries will fly to Washington. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Japanese government, in view of the fact that China has sent Song Ziwen to attend the economic conference, with the apparent intention of lobbying various countries to raise the Manchurian issue, attaches great importance to this delicate international relationship. Important instructions will be issued to Representative Ishii. The Army also held a meeting of its leaders in the minister's office yesterday afternoon to discuss countermeasures in case the Manchurian issue is raised, focusing on issuing instructions to Representative Ishii and has already decided on the outline. (20th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Japan Collects National Wealth to Prevent Economic Blockade

(Tokyo) It is rumored here that the Japanese government, in view of the possibility that member states may take economic blockade measures against Japan after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, has ordered various ministries to prepare a legal bill within the scope of their duties. This bill stipulates that once an economic blockade is implemented, all of Japan's national wealth will be collected to deal with it. Japanese newspapers have all published this news. (19th Havas Dispatch)

Dutch Parliament Asks for Attention to Actions of Japanese in Dutch Territories

Circumstances of the Establishment of the Dutch-Japanese Arbitration Treaty

The Hague During the discussion of the Dutch East Indies budget in the Dutch Upper House today, Socialist Member Dr. Munter asked for attention to the fact that Japan currently needs oil from the East Indies for its warships and wants to establish a Japanese settlement on New Guinea Island, which is of dubious intent. Colonial Minister Graaf replied that the government is currently very cautious and applies all laws applicable to other countries to Japan. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

The Hague The Dutch-Japanese Arbitration Treaty was signed today, providing for the establishment of a conciliation committee. If there are any disputes, they should be submitted to the Permanent Court or the Arbitration Court. In view of the impact of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations on its membership in the Permanent Court, both parties agreed to continue discussions on this point. Japan hopes that this treaty can serve as a model for concluding treaties with other countries so that Japan will not be isolated after withdrawing from the League of Nations. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Foreign Ministry announced the circumstances of the establishment of the Dutch-Japanese Arbitration Treaty at noon today as follows: In 1925, the Dutch government expressed its hope to conclude a treaty on arbitration and continued negotiations until now. The Imperial Government decided on the outline of the policy to conclude the treaty at the Cabinet meeting on the 14th. On the 19th, the signing ceremony was held by Saito, the Japanese Minister to the Netherlands, and Blokland, the Dutch Foreign Minister. This treaty symbolizes the cordial relations between the Netherlands and Japan for three centuries. The main points of the content are as follows: 1. This treaty stipulates mediation and arbitration. All disputes that cannot be resolved by diplomatic means will be submitted to a permanent mediation committee for a resolution. The resolution is not binding on the two governments. 1. The mediation committee is composed of five members. After the treaty is implemented, the two countries will negotiate to appoint the members. 1. Legal disputes, with the consent of both countries, will be submitted to arbitration for resolution. The arbitration will be carried out by the Hague Court of Justice or by an arbitration tribunal established by agreement between the two countries. There will be five judges. 1. This treaty will take effect after the exchange of ratification and will be valid for five years. (20th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

India-Japan Commercial Treaty Cancelled

Japan's Boycott of Indian Cotton is Fierce in Appearance But Weak in Reality

Bombay According to an investigation by the authorities, Japan has already shipped all its cotton textile inventory for this year to the Indian market and is not at all troubled by the new 50% tax rate. This tax rate has been revised five times since 1930. It is generally believed that Japan will boycott Indian cotton as soon as it has sold all its dumped goods. India's cotton exports to Japan amount to 90 million Japanese yen annually. The local cotton industry has already been stirred up and is rumored to be boycotting Japanese goods. (20th Havas Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Japan Cotton Textile and Drug Union Federation and the Export Cotton Textile Trade Association Federation today discussed countermeasures for the cancellation of the Japan-India Trade Treaty. As a result, they issued the following strong statement: 1. Implement a ban on the sale of Indian cotton. 1. Impose the highest tax rate on Japanese goods and also impose the same amount of import tariffs on Indian cotton. (20th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

United States Abandons Gold Standard

Announces Restoration of Gold Export Embargo

Domestic Prices Already Soaring

Roosevelt Decides to Stop Maintaining Gold Parity

Will Request Congress to Grant Authority to Inflate Currency

Aiming to Use as Powerful Weapon in Future Economic Talks

National News Agency, Washington, 19th "The United States has now abandoned the gold standard." This straightforward statement was made by US Treasury Secretary Woodin at the end of the world's fiercest currency war. This war had lasted for a long time, and at one point, it had caused the value of the US dollar to depreciate to 92 cents against other currencies.

Reuters, Washington, 19th President Roosevelt declared today that the restoration of the cash export ban is a way to raise domestic prices. Treasury Secretary Woodin, in response to questions, said that the United States has indeed temporarily suspended the gold standard and is not issuing export licenses for gold. Meanwhile, he announced the previously specified regulations for permitted cash exports. Woodin declined to elaborate on the regulations, but said that when they are issued, it will be clear what can be exported and what cannot. It is speculated in some quarters that cash used to settle commercial contracts entered into before this week may still be licensed for export.

Reuters, Washington, 19th Senator Thomas and government advisors have drafted an amendment to the rural relief bill to grant President Roosevelt greater power to inflate the currency. It is reported that the President has agreed to this amendment. The bill is expected to be submitted to Congress today. In addition to authorizing the President to issue currency at his discretion, it also stipulates that debtor countries may use silver to repay war debts under certain conditions, and that the gold content of the US dollar may be reduced through international agreements or other means.

Havas, Washington, 20th President Roosevelt's decision to prohibit cash exports, that is, to abandon the gold standard, is due to Congress's urgent desire to raise prices and its intention to pass unrestricted currency inflation policies, even if it is not timely. Under these circumstances, much of the effectiveness of Roosevelt's discussions with British Prime Minister MacDonald and French representative Herriot on economic and monetary issues will be lost, because the conclusions that can be reached in the three-nation talks will be overturned by the US House of Representatives or Senate. Roosevelt believes that the best way to achieve results in the three-nation talks is to let the US dollar rise and fall naturally in the foreign market, but to control it when necessary. It is said that the President's move, if regarded as a threat to countries with low exchange rates, to facilitate economic negotiations, is a misunderstanding. The President's move is specifically to avoid disorderly currency inflation. In short, the purpose of this policy is to enable countries with devalued currencies to conclude an agreement at the end of the economic conference to restore the gold standard.

National News Agency, Washington, 19th Since the US Treasury Secretary announced that the United States had officially abandoned the gold standard, from financial leaders to the poorest farmers, everyone has been seized by a frenzy of currency inflation. Tonight, the US government has obtained the full support of the nation's largest banks to begin a currency inflation plan. It is expected that within 48 hours, Congress will transfer its constitutional power to the President, allowing him to inflate the US dollar, reuse silver as currency, devalue the gold dollar, and negotiate with foreign countries to stabilize global exchange rates, and accept no more than 100 million yuan of silver from debtor countries. It is also heard that this revaluation of the gold dollar and reuse of silver as currency will be an important objective of the United States at the World Economic Conference.

National News Agency, Washington, 19th Official opinion is that the United States abandoned the gold standard when the Treasury Department initially announced that it would no longer maintain the value of the gold dollar with gold exports, allowing it to rise and fall naturally. The US government's decision to stop maintaining the value of the gold dollar is due to President Roosevelt's efforts to raise prices. Although the President has not yet issued a formal statement on the reaffirmation of the gold ban, White House officials have confirmed this, saying that the President wants to raise prices through the passive method of no longer maintaining the value of the gold dollar. Therefore, he specially issued an executive order prohibiting the export of gold, only gold already labeled as foreign-owned and the balance due in trade settlements may be exported in accordance with previous regulations. As a result, prices in the domestic market soared, and stock prices also surged. Silver prices in the metal trade rose the most sharply, reaching the maximum limit allowed by exchange regulations, rising to 300 pounds. Rubber, silk, and grains also experienced similar sharp increases. Only sugar prices were not greatly affected and failed to rise as sharply as other commodities, and sales volumes also decreased significantly. Operators said that they are currently groping for a way forward and it is difficult to make a judgment for the time being. At this time, the opinions of financiers and economic experts are very confused. A group in New York demanded that Woodin immediately announce the Treasury Department's future policy, whether it will actually abandon the maintenance of the gold dollar's value, or only temporarily abandon it. But the only response from the White House was to announce that gold exports would be prohibited until further notice. This situation led officials to admit that the United States had abandoned the gold standard. Currently, rumors about this move are rampant. In New York, it is rumored that the President wants to ban all gold exports, even those listed as exceptions in the executive order, in preparation for currency inflation. However, inquiries to government offices have not been able to confirm this. Congress is quite troubled by the status of the gold dollar in the foreign market. Several congressmen have pointed out that its value may not be stable, and that maintaining it is futile. The general supporters of currency inflation are also meeting urgently. It is rumored that these people have sent a letter to the President, stating that if the White House does not immediately prepare all practical plans, Congress will pass its own inflation plan. However, this cannot be confirmed at present. Only Senator Thomas, who met with the President yesterday, said that he hoped that an important statement would be issued in 24 hours. When the excitement subsided slightly, economic experts and those close to the President said that they expected the President to ask Congress to grant him more discretionary power on monetary issues in order to control the situation. Several congressmen also said that although this is tantamount to Congress abandoning its constitutional right to coin money and regulate its value, many congressmen support abandoning this right in an emergency, so that the President can be given a powerful weapon when discussing economic matters with other countries. A leader of the Democratic Party said that even if Congress grants this power to the President, it is not expected that the President will use it, but only to protect the policies of the United States in future talks. This is its main result. As for opening the path to immediate and large-scale currency inflation, it is not the real purpose.

Government Drafts Currency Inflation Bill

National News Agency, Washington, 19th The currency inflation bill drafted by US Treasury Secretary Woodin, Secretary of State Hull, and other key figures will include the following four points: 1. The President will independently initiate the revaluation of the gold dollar through the use of silver as currency and other best methods; 2. Negotiate agreements with foreign countries to revalue gold and stabilize currencies; 3. When the President deems it necessary, he may print greenbacks (note name) or other forms of currency; 4. Accept silver from debtor countries at a price not exceeding 50 cents per ounce, not exceeding 100 million yuan. While the US government is busy drafting this new bill, the head of J.P. Morgan & Co. also issued a statement in New York, endorsing the President's measures, stating that it is now clear that all efforts to maintain the exchange rate of the US gold dollar, keeping currencies devalued by other countries at a premium, has had a contractionary effect on the currency, resulting in a contraction of US prices and wages, and increasing unemployment. Therefore, I feel that the clear path to escaping economic recession is to overcome this deflationary force, and that the government's current measures are the best path under the current circumstances.

Friends of the President said that Roosevelt may not be forced to use all the powers granted by this bill, especially regarding printing greenbacks or currency without fixed gold or silver reserves. The purpose is only to obtain greater power, so that he can conclude favorable agreements with countries such as Britain and France. When asking other countries to raise their currency exchange rates, he can use the possibility of depreciating the US currency and putting it in a competitive position as a bargaining chip. Most White House advisors also said that the saying that this move will give the President a powerful bargaining weapon is not entirely accurate, because in fact this new power will enable the United States to respond to many proposals made by other countries. As for the attitude of Congress towards this bill, according to the joint statement of various leaders, it is expected to be passed.

Abandoning the Gold Standard Has Four Effects

Reuters, New York, 20th The New York Tribune stated that President Roosevelt's formal abandonment of the gold standard has

Page 7

four effects: 1. To raise domestic prices to suit the world situation; 2. To facilitate the expansion of domestic lending without the need to artificially maintain the price of the US dollar abroad; 3. To improve the position of the United States in dealing with monetary issues with other countries at the Washington pre-meeting of the World Economic Conference; 4. To curb the tendency of uncontrolled inflation plans in Congress. Speakers have different opinions on the US President's policies, but most agree with what the Tribune said. It is expected that the meaning of the US President's policies can be seen in the attachments to the rural relief bill. It is now heard that the plan agreed to by Roosevelt will give the President full power to handle the national currency. It is said that the current gold content of the US dollar is 23.22 grains, and it will be reduced to 16 grains in the future. The amendment proposed by Senator Thomas, which can be submitted to the Senate today, is heard to stipulate that the President has the power to determine currency inflation. Therefore, if appropriate, the President will naturally have the power to reduce the gold content. From the phenomenon, the World Economic Conference may discuss the possibility of revising the current 40% standard of the currency gold ratio. The US authorities are obviously unwilling to agree to Congress's proposal to broadly mint silver coins, or plans similar to those proposed by former Senator Bryan. According to the most reliable sources, the government will have a way to deal with silver, but at the same time, it will strictly limit the use of silver as the basis of the currency.

Speculative Frenzy, Market Suddenly Active

Reuters, New York, 19th When the stock exchange opened today, prices were up one to eleven pounds. At the close, many securities were up one to eight pounds. News that a currency inflation plan was being considered in Washington was met with a feverish frenzy by speculators. The stock-buying activity was unprecedented since September last year. Industrial stocks also rose, and trading was very active. Prudent people said that when Britain suspended cash payments, the price of the pound first soared and then plummeted. The past is a guide for the future, so be careful. But this statement is not enough to suppress the courage of speculators. The restoration of the gold ban made the US dollar hopeless, and foreign exchange rates soared. Government bonds tended to weaken due to the development of inflation, while other securities were lively, especially foreign bonds were firm. Major bankers today expressed great hope for the government's decision to handle the inflation issue. The people of the country expect the government to take decisive action to stop the painful and seemingly endless process of tightening. After the commodity market received the news that the government would adopt an inflationary process, it suddenly became active. The buying of grains was frantic, which was rare in peacetime. The Chicago wheat market initially rose by five cents per bushel, but near the close, many closed out positions, causing the already increased price to fall a lot, but it was still one and seventy-five to two and a half cents higher than yesterday. The cotton market rose by about two dollars per bale. The market price of silver bars also rose to the highest level since November 1931. At the same time, rubber, cowhide, and silk all reached heights not seen in recent years. Speculative buying spread throughout the markets, so the number of transactions was mostly a new record. Spot silver rose by three and a half cents today due to speculators' unbridled buying, which was the largest increase in many years. Silver futures also soared, reaching a maximum of three cents, which is also a rare spectacle since the establishment of the metal exchange. Silver futures later fell due to closing out positions, but soon rose again. All monthly futures were about three cents higher than the previous day. The silver market has this increase because silver will occupy an important part in a practical currency inflation plan.

War News Obtained in Zunhua

Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya.

Talks with Chief of Staff Zhang and Deputy Army Commander Qin

Special Dispatch from Zunhua: The 29th Army, which accepted the critical situation of the retreat of the Jehol Army and stubbornly defended Xifengkou in hard fighting, refreshing international views, has its headquarters in Zunhua. Army Commander Song Zheyuan is in Tianjin for medical treatment. Deputy Commander-in-Chief Qin Dechun and the division commanders are commanding on the front lines. The reporter specifically visited Chief of Staff Zhang, whose conversation was as follows: "The national war to protect the country and defend the people is the only excellent opportunity that our soldiers have encountered in 21 years, and it is also the honorable and natural duty that our soldiers hope to fulfill. We are very grateful for the comfort from the people, but we dare not take it for granted. Our army has been fighting hard against Japan for more than a month. The Japanese army took our superior positions first and has new and sharp weapons, so our army's casualties have reached nearly 6,000. However, we do not begrudge it, and no one has ever complained. This is in accordance with the Army Commander's usual training of 'advance without retreat, die without regret.' We deeply feel that if we do not fight to the death, it will not only damage the national character, but also be impossible to face people. Our soldiers have no face to wear military uniforms. Because the government is constrained by the Communist Party, it is difficult to transfer elite troops to continue to support the north for a while. Therefore, our army insists on the determination of the greatest sacrifice. Even if only one soldier is left, we are willing to seek benevolence and obtain benevolence. If it is possible, we must preserve a bit of vitality for the country. It is indeed a pity and painful to consume too much useful flesh and blood. However, at this time when the enemy's flames are spreading and constantly forcing us, if we retreat step by step, how can we bear it? When the violent Japan first occupied the three northeastern provinces, its heart was not only in the three northeastern provinces. Now that it is attacking Chahar and Hebei, its wild ambitions are more than just North China. The country has sown evil causes and evil results due to years of civil war. At this time, we should thoroughly understand and dispel the misunderstanding and unite to face the outside world." Then the reporter told him that the villagers along the way mostly asked about the news of the planes. Zhang replied, "The soldiers on the front line, because of the enemy's fierce bombing, when they cannot withstand the bombing, also think like the old people who are concerned about the war. The other day, the enemy deputy army commander met with Minister He in Beiping, and was sincerely concerned about the fierce bombing by Japanese planes. Our deputy army commander smiled and replied, 'Fortunately, in the war of the 19th year, we had tasted the taste of planes, so we are also calm.' The bombs dropped by the enemy planes are about the height of one person, and the range of the explosion is about 10 meters, and the depth of the soil is 3 meters. The loss of the bombed position is very large. Our army was reorganized into the 11th Division in the 19th year, and reduced to three divisions. Under special circumstances, the remaining officers and soldiers had to find ways to provide them with rations. The resources are limited, and there is no way to economize on the expenses. The army is extremely poor. Each soldier needs one and a half catties of flour per day on weekdays. During the war, the consumption is more than one and a half catties. According to the regulations, we will not be able to afford it. Therefore, in the past 30 days or so, the rations issued to the soldiers have only been slightly more than usual, and not enough for wartime. It is really unavoidable. The failure of Jehol was first and foremost due to the lack of cooperation between the soldiers and the people. We have heard songs everywhere, which is a warning. Our army usually does not harm the people in the slightest. The food and grass supplied by the people in the war zone are recorded in detail, and when the funds arrive, they will be repaid one by one. Fortunately, we have the trust of the people, and they give us assistance, which is enough to encourage our soldiers at the front. We must have today, and we will have the future. We will never repeat the mistake of opening the door to welcome the bandits. We must implement our determination to 'advance without retreat, die without regret.'" Later, the reporter asked about the recent war situation. He said that the deputy army commander would return from the front line at night, and there would be news to tell. Let's make another appointment for a chat. The reporter then resigned.

At 8:00 a.m. today (16th), I went to the army headquarters and met Chief of Staff Zhang. He said that Deputy Army Commander Qin had returned and was going to Beiping. I was immediately invited into a small room for soldiers. Deputy Army Commander Qin then came out to meet me and said that years of civil war have led to economic backwardness and rural bankruptcy, which has given Japanese imperialism the opportunity to intensify its aggression. Recently, its wild ambitions have become even more blatant. Our army had long anticipated today's serious national crisis, so we have always taken protecting the country and defending the people and thoroughly resisting imperialism as military training. Knowing yourself and knowing your enemy, you can win a hundred battles. The enemy has new and sharp weapons, which are certainly advantageous for daytime warfare and long-range warfare. Although our weapons are not as good as theirs, we can use night warfare and close warfare, that is, at night, we can surprise the enemy and wield a large sword to chop off the enemy's heads. The war situation last month has been detailed in various newspapers. From the 9th of this month to today, the positions have been repeatedly gained and lost, and the enemy and we have suddenly advanced and retreated, all engaging in fierce hand-to-hand combat. The 12th day and the first half of the 13th day were the most intense. Our officers and soldiers suffered 500 to 600 casualties. Yesterday, the enemy army waded across the Sa River and occupied two small villages on our right flank, one named Nantuanting and the other named Beituanting. We wounded one battalion commander, killed two company commanders, and wounded and killed more than 100 soldiers. However, at night, the two villages were taken back by our army's desperate efforts. In this nearly 40-day war of resistance against Japan, the lessons learned are: 1. Scientific inventions, of course, flesh and blood cannot resist guns and bullets, but if the people of the country are rich in patriotism and sacrifice, and if they can add sufficient material, it would be even better. Otherwise, the spirit may not be able to overcome matter. 2. It is important to use our strengths to attack the enemy's weaknesses. The enemy's strengths must be prevented from being brought into play, and our weaknesses must be properly protected. 3. Dispatching reinforcements must be flexible and fast, especially for marching on foot in inconvenient transportation. 4. The division lies in harmony. The entire army is under a single commander, regardless of boundaries. The divisions should be like family fathers and sons, responding to each other's attacks, and striving towards a common goal. 5. This is an international war, also known as modern three-dimensional warfare. The entire nation, soldiers and civilians, should be mobilized in unison. The army is an effective force for the people, and the people are a strong support for the army. Most of our army's achievements come from the help and encouragement of the people. The wounded soldiers abandoned on the battlefield are often risked by the villagers to carry them back. When there are traces of the enemy, they will report them. The Zunhua militia firmly requested to participate in the work on the front lines, which is a glimpse. Other material and spiritual assistance given by the people in various places is beyond description. Since the beginning of the war of resistance, about 5,000 soldiers have died. The usual ratio of war casualties is 7 to 3, but now, because the weapons are not as good as others, the casualty rate is 6 to 4, and there is a danger of exceeding it," and so on. Later, the reporter firmly requested to go to the front line for inspection. He introduced Division Commanders Zhang Zizhong, Liu Ruming, and Shen Kesan, and their wives who fought with the army, and made brief talks. They all agreed to go to the front line for inspection tonight. The reporter and a total of seven people stood in the courtyard, laughing and talking to each other, as if forgetting the hardships of the battlefield. They took a photo and dispersed. Today, at 3:00 or 4:00 p.m., I faintly heard the rumble of artillery fire. The residents all went to the dug-out openings to listen to prevent planes, but it has not yet been confirmed where the artillery fire came from. (16th)

Fuzhou National Salvation Association Implements Joint Responsibility System

Merchants of All Guilds Must Not Promote Enemy Goods

Three People Form a Group to Supervise and Report Each Other

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since the reorganization of the Automatic National Salvation Association in this city, it has been extremely enthusiastic about boycotting enemy goods. In addition to sealing up all old inferior goods from various guilds and not allowing them to be sold, it also telegraphed the merchants in Hong Kong and Shanghai that if they send goods to Fujian in the future, they must obtain a certificate from the original manufacturer for inspection. If any false or counterfeit goods are discovered, the merchant should be responsible. Therefore, inferior goods have gradually disappeared from the market in Fuzhou recently, and imports have also greatly decreased. However, the Automatic National Salvation Association is still afraid that unscrupulous merchants may secretly transport and sell them, undermining the overall situation, so it has implemented a joint responsibility system (with three households forming a group) to supervise and report each other to eliminate malpractices. The full text of the 21 articles of the joint responsibility system is copied below:

Article 1: This association aims to fully express the spirit of the people's automatic national salvation and to take effective actions for national salvation by implementing a joint guarantee system. This Joint Responsibility System (hereinafter referred to as "this System") is specifically formulated. Article 2: This System applies to business entities, commercial intermediaries, or business employees who implement automatic national salvation. Article 3: This System may be applied mutatis mutandis to manual laborers or intellectual laborers who implement automatic national salvation. Article 4: Those who accept the constraints of this System have the absolute obligation to abide by the covenant in Article 5 of the same System. Article 5: The covenant of this System is as follows: 1. Do not promote goods manufactured by enemy countries. 2. Do not purchase goods produced by enemy countries. 3. Do not provide enemy countries with the food they need. 4. Do not supply raw materials for enemy countries' military supplies. 5. Do not transport enemy countries' goods. 6. Do not provide labor or intelligence services to the people of enemy countries. 7. Do not engage in any other acts that are beneficial to enemy countries. Article 6: Those who accept the constraints of this System and violate any of the items listed in Article 5 of the same System shall be deemed to have violated the covenant. Article 7: When those who accept the constraints of this System commit acts of violating the covenant, they shall be punished in accordance with the punishment methods listed in Article 8 of the same System, depending on the severity of the circumstances. Article 8: The punishment methods of this System are as follows: 1. Confiscation, 2. Suspension of business, 3. Detention, 4. Parade through the streets, 5. Standing in a cage, 6. Cutting off the ears, 7. Execution. Article 9: Business entities that accept the constraints of this System shall be linked together in groups of three shops and shall be jointly responsible for supervision and mutual reporting. Article 10: In the same group, if one shop or one person violates the covenant, the other two shops or two persons shall be responsible for reporting and shall have the obligation to report. Article 11: When the person responsible for reporting discovers that a related person in the same group has violated the covenant, he shall report to this association in writing or orally. Article 12: If a related person in the same group has committed an act of violating the covenant, and the person responsible for reporting knows about it but does not report it, he shall be deemed an accomplice and shall be subject to an appropriate punishment. Article 13: Business employees who accept the constraints of this System have the obligation to report the violation of the covenant by the business entity of their respective shops. Article 14: Business employees who accept the constraints of this System and fail to report the violation of the covenant by the business entity of their respective shops shall be subject to an appropriate punishment. Article 15: Those who accept the constraints of this System may conduct inspections on the shops of related persons in the same group at any time. Article 16: When those who accept the constraints of this System refuse the inspection of a related person in the same group, the related person shall report to this association. Article 17: The person responsible for reporting may request this association to keep his secret when necessary. Article 18: Those who accept the constraints of this System shall fill out a voluntary application to accept the joint responsibility system and shall be jointly guaranteed by the related persons in the same group (the format of the voluntary application shall be determined separately). Article 19: When those who are bound by this Joint Responsibility System are reported to have violated the covenant, the execution committee shall execute it after the judgment of the arbitration committee of this association. Article 20: This Joint Responsibility System shall be implemented after being resolved and passed by the Fuzhou Community Representatives Conference. Article 21: Matters not covered by this Joint Responsibility System may be revised by the Representatives Conference at any time. (17th)

Yu Guocai's Troops Returned to Guizhou from Yunnan

After Several Mediations by Long Yun and Others

Wang Jialie Allotted Defense Areas to Yu

Chongqing Correspondence: After Wang Jialie returned to Guiyang in Guizhou Province, Yu Guocai went to Beijing to seek assistance, and then went to Yunnan Province to ask Yunnan Province Chairman Long Yun to send troops to help restore the situation in Guizhou, willing to cede ten counties as a reward. Long and Yu were originally on the same front, and he was quite willing, but Long was also afraid of being dissatisfied by Guangdong and Guangxi, so he changed his plan to become a mediator for Yu and Wang, instructing Yu to gather about 5,000 remnants of Wei and Wu on the border of Yunnan Province, and the military rations were temporarily supplied by Yunnan Province to maintain the status quo. On the one hand, he telegraphed Wang Jialie, asking him to give Yu's troops appropriate arrangements to avoid other changes. At that time, Wang Jialie had not yet resolved the situation of Che Mingyi's troops in the east, and Hou Zhidan's troops in the north were also in close contact with Mao Guangxiang, so he had many concerns. However, on the surface, he still refused to show weakness and refused to accept Long Yun's proposition. Therefore, Yu Guocai became very angry and immediately appointed Wu Jianping as the commander of the advance troops, and he himself took office as the commander-in-chief, leading 5,000 troops to attack Xingyi, Anlong and other counties. Wang then sent Li Chengzhang's brigade and He Zhizhong's division to meet the enemy, and the two sides came into contact near Xingyi. At the same time, the anti-Wang atmosphere in Guizhou Province took the opportunity to become strong. Wang Jialie felt that the environment was not good. The actual strength of his troops was only about 10,000, scattered throughout Guizhou, which was not enough. There was no ability to start a war. He had no choice but to send Mao Yueqiu to Kunming to meet Long Yun, asking him to convey to Yu Guocai to stop military actions and discuss peaceful solutions together. Long Yun immediately responded to his request, and the tense Guizhou war was eased. Yu Guocai also went to Luoping to discuss everything with He Zhizhong. As a result of the peace talks, Wang Jialie welcomed Yu Guocai back to Guizhou and allotted three counties, including Xingyi and Anlong, for Yu's troops to temporarily garrison, and allocated 50,000 yuan per month in military salaries to support Yu's troops. A scene of turmoil finally subsided. However, Yu believed that with 5,000 troops and the territory of three counties, it was difficult to distribute them, so he telegraphed Wang Jialie again, stating that the return of his troops to Guizhou was a temporary garrison. Once there was a suitable opportunity, he would lead his troops north to resist Japan and requested that the eight counties of Panjiang be allotted to him as well. Initially, Wang Jialie did not agree, believing that allotting the eight counties of Panjiang to Yu's army, together with the three counties of Xingyi and others, would total eleven counties. The defense area would be wide, and in the future, Yu's troops would become powerful and would inevitably raise troops to force him to resign. After Mao Yueqiu, Lu Shouchi, Long Yun, and others tried their best to mediate, Wang finally agreed. The allotment has now been officially made, and Yu's troops have also entered and garrisoned separately. (April 18)

He Chengjun Goes to Jiangxi to Meet Chiang Kai-shek for Instructions

He Jian Appointed Bandit Suppression Commissioner for the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Border Region

Hankou Correspondence: He Jian, Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army, recently attended the Seven Provinces Security Conference in Nanchang. Having completed his duties, he flew to Hankou on the 18th from Xunyang. Xu Yuanquan, Commander of the Tenth Army, also participated in the discussions. Arrangements and coordination between the armies of the two provinces were decided, along with a resolution to eliminate regional boundaries and act uniformly. After the plan is finalized, the two Hes will instruct their respective troops to strictly follow it. He Jian left Hankou on the 20th by the Wuchang-Changsha railway to return to Hunan. Zheng Yuxiu Case:

Investigating Cha Laisheng

Request to Disqualify Judges Rejected

Zheng Yuxiu, the former president of the Shanghai District Court, was impeached by the Supervisory Yuan for dereliction of duty and embezzlement. The case was transferred to the Jiangning District Court by the Jiangsu High Court for investigation and prosecution. Currently, Cha Laisheng has submitted a request to the Jiangsu High Procuratorate to disqualify the judge presiding over the case. Wang Simo, the chief procurator of the High Procuratorate, rejected the request, stating that only parties involved in the case are entitled to request disqualification, as clearly stipulated in the Criminal Procedure Law. Furthermore, since the case has already been prosecuted, there is no basis for disqualification. Therefore, yesterday (the 20th), a notice was issued rejecting Cha Laisheng's request as being contrary to the law.

Jiang Hong's Second Appeal Case Concluded

Jiang Hong, director of the Jiangyin County Relief Institute, was accused by Ji Sha of Jiangyin County of defrauding her of five thousand yuan on suspicion of her son Ji Renhua being a counter-revolutionary. The Jiangyin County Government sentenced Jiang to a fine of two hundred yuan. Jiang filed a second appeal, which upheld the original verdict. He then filed a third appeal, which was referred to the Wuxian District Court for retrial. The court held a hearing at 3 p.m. yesterday (the 20th). Jiang hired lawyers Zhang Yipeng and Tang Ying for his defense, while Ji Sha hired lawyer Zhang Shiying. Jiang claimed that the five thousand yuan was not obtained through fraud, but given by Ji Sha to ease tensions. Three thousand yuan was used to purchase firearms for the Public Security Bureau, and two thousand yuan was a charitable donation to the Relief Institute. Ji Sha claimed that the county government did not receive the three thousand yuan, and Jiang pocketed the two thousand yuan. After the lawyers' arguments, the court scheduled sentencing for the 26th.

Petition to Levy Additional Land Tax

One Kidnapper Killed

Ling Xichun's son Jicheng, eleven years old, a resident of Tuanwu near Xialiqiao in Shaoxing, was kidnapped by bandits who sent a letter demanding ransom. Page 8

Local News

Mayor Wu Issues Statement Yesterday

Opposing Concessions Seizing Factory Inspection

But Still Willing to Negotiate with Concession Authorities

Central News Agency reports: Regarding the passage by Western taxpayers in the Public Concession the other day of amendments to the Yangjingbang Regulations, Annex, to seize factory inspection rights, Mayor Wu issued the following statement:

I have stated that factory inspection, regarding our country's entire labor administration and the enforcement of factory law in the concession, should belong to Chinese government agencies. There is absolutely no reason to object to this claim by the Chinese government, whether based on political principles, legal principles, or the powers of the Municipal Council itself. However, the Municipal Council continues its practice of exploiting amendments to the Yangjingbang Regulations or adding annexes to wantonly expand its powers, a practice that anyone familiar with the history of concession development cannot but regret. Yesterday, when Chairman Bell of the Municipal Council read the motion, he did say that the reason why the Municipal Council could not inspect factories was due to historical reasons. I firmly believe that if Chairman Bell considered the entire history of concession development, his views would certainly change. In July 1862, when the Shanghai Daotai wanted to levy taxes on Chinese people in the concession, the British consul objected, but British Minister Bruce instructed the British consul, "The treaty does not allow us to interfere in this matter. The Daotai should have the right to levy taxes on Chinese, which are already paid by residents both inside and outside the city beyond the concession. We have no reason to object." He also said, "If we do not allow the Chinese government to govern the Chinese people in the concession, then we cannot rely on Article 18 of the treaty for protection from the government and people of that country." The British Minister's opinion was supported by the British government. Therefore, the following year, British Foreign Secretary Russell informed the British Minister, "The land of the British concession undoubtedly belongs to China. The fact that Chinese people live in the concession does not exempt them from their obligations to that country." At that time, some foreigners in Shanghai were still unaware of this, so the British Minister instructed the British consul, "The Chinese government has never formally given up its right to govern the Chinese people, and the British government has never requested or clearly expressed any desire to obtain the right to protect the Chinese people. Please do not forget these two matters. The British government is unwilling to maintain a system that cannot stand on principle." The British Minister's attitude was supported by all countries. American Minister Balingen instructed American Consul Seward, "Foreigners often infringe on the rights of Chinese people when managing municipal affairs. Therefore, foreigners must be awakened to return to the safe zone of principle. I cannot agree to any method that disregards China's rights, that is, the rights that a sovereign state should have over its land and people." In summary, the legal status of the concession is very clear. Even historically, the limitations on the powers of the Municipal Council are self-evident. We must not forget our origins. The Municipal Council knows full well that even according to the Yangjingbang Land Regulations, which were painstakingly and meticulously developed by its predecessors, the Municipal Council has no right to manage factory affairs. It also knows that any attempt to amend the regulations for this purpose will not be agreed to by the Chinese government. Therefore, it seeks to use a trick, based on Article 11 of the regulations, to convene a special meeting of Western taxpayers to amend the annex, hoping that after the motion is passed, it will be approved by more than half of the consuls and ministers of the treaty countries, and thus be effective without the consent of the Chinese government. This is clearly feigning ignorance. The same article of the regulations stipulates that any additions, alterations, or terminations must not conflict with the regulations. According to the Yangjingbang Regulations, the so-called fundamental law of the concession, its powers are limited to the following: first, to establish a public bureau; second, to construct and maintain various necessary projects within the concession; third, to properly manage and clean the entire concession, establish street lights, store water to sprinkle the ground to prevent dust, and open ditches; fourth, to establish street patrols and police (this was added later; initially, only watchmen could be established); fifth, to prepare public land and buildings required by the public bureau, either by renting or buying; sixth, to raise funds for the officials and staff required by the public bureau. Therefore, Article 9 of the Municipal Council Regulations, which states that "the concession area must be prepared for governance to ensure its proper management," lists the matters that are permitted to be governed, and is not a comprehensive list. According to the established rules of legal interpretation, the difference between a listed method and a comprehensive method is that the former is limited to the items listed, while the latter can be analogized. The purpose of adding annexes is only to achieve "the various items of the regulations can be made more perfect," but cannot go beyond the scope of the items listed in the regulations. Otherwise, it would conflict with the provision in Article 11 of the regulations that "it cannot be contrary to the regulations," and would be invalid. Therefore, the motion passed yesterday by the Western taxpayers' meeting regarding factory inspection cannot obtain a legal basis according to the Yangjingbang Regulations. I deeply regret the Municipal Council's adoption of this attitude. However, the Chinese government will never give up its right to the entire labor administration, let alone the concession authorities' attempt to seize our country's labor administration rights, which has no legal basis. Its position and the passing of the annex are no different from before. However, factory management is a matter of urgency that cannot be delayed. I am still willing to sincerely negotiate with the concession authorities to find a solution that does not infringe on Chinese sovereignty and at the same time benefits all the city's workers and promotes harmonious labor-management relations.

Ma Zhanshan Cables Arrival in Poland

Over Ten Thousand Troops Return Home in Batches

Ma Zhanshan, the Northeast anti-Japanese general who retreated into the Soviet Union, cabled various parties in Beijing and Shanghai yesterday, reporting that he and 66 other senior generals, such as Su Bingwen, Li Du, and Wang Delin, arrived in Moscow on the 18th. Yan Huiqing, our country's ambassador to Russia, personally welcomed them at the station, providing food and expressing deep gratitude. After a short rest, they left Moscow and set off to return home, arriving safely in Poland on the 19th. They are expected to arrive in Germany on the 22nd. Whether they will transfer through France or take a ship back home from Germany will be decided after arriving in Germany. However, their hearts are set on returning home as soon as possible, to go to the front lines again to kill the enemy and save the country. Over 10,000 troops who retreated into Russia were disarmed in Russia and then departed in batches to return to Xinjiang, our country. The first batch of over 2,000 people has already arrived in Xinjiang Province, the second batch of over 3,000 people is currently en route, and the third batch of 5,000 people has also begun to depart. It is expected that they will all arrive in Xinjiang within a month.

Reuters, Berlin, April 20: General Ma Zhanshan and his party of sixty people arrived here today. Most of the men are dressed in Western suits, but the women and children are still dressed in Chinese attire, so when the train arrived at the Penkof station, everyone scrambled to see them, regarding it as a spectacle. Ma Zhanshan and others are currently refusing to disclose the details of the battle. They will stay here briefly before returning home.

US Abolition of Gold Standard Does Not Affect This City

National News Agency reports: Yesterday, the United States abolished the gold standard and simultaneously reinstated the gold embargo to prevent an extreme outflow of gold, causing a great change in the gold industry in this city. The gold exchange fell sharply from the morning, with the standard gold price, which had previously broken the 1,000 yuan mark, falling below 1,000 yuan. The market was chaotic, with a difference of over sixty taels between the morning and afternoon. The reporter specially inquired about the details from a financial giant in the financial sector, as follows:

US Abolishes Gold Standard

It was said that the US suddenly abolished the gold standard, which it has always used, and it is impossible to predict future changes. However, the reason for its abolition is certainly no more than insufficient reserves due to high production. There are also relations in auxiliary currency. The US use gold coins, like our use silver dollar. If we only used silver dollars and had no bronze coins and small silver coins as supplements, circulation would be inconvenient. The situation in the US's abolishing the gold standard is certainly not that simple. In short, it can be said that there is no harm to China, and even some benefit.

Beneficial to China

As for the claim that it is beneficial, it is because after the US abolishes the gold standard, it will use silver. In this way, the price of gold will fall and the price of silver will rise. China has always used silver, and its annual imports exceed its exports. Now, using the same amount of silver, we can buy more goods, which is beneficial. Exporters must clearly lose, but in recent years, the customs records show that imports exceed exports in almost every month. Simultaneously Implemented Gold Embargo

The US's abandonment of the gold standard and simultaneous restoration of the gold embargo is also a matter of course. The US is afraid that after gold is converted to silver, it will be useless for a while and will flow out too much, which is not beneficial to the US. Therefore, it must be exported. China is currently valued in silver dollars, but it is still under a gold embargo. Increasing Purchasing Power

The original intention of the US's abandonment of the gold standard, in my observation, is that domestic production is congested, and the supply of all goods exceeds demand. The people are limited by their high standard of living, especially with the implementation of the gold standard. On the one hand, the people cannot afford it, and on the other hand, finance becomes stagnant. Merchants cannot sell their goods and deposit them all in banks. The banks turn cash into dead goods, finance is not smooth, and so on. Therefore, this measure is taken. After its implementation, not only will finance circulate, but the people will be able to reduce their expenses and slightly increase their purchasing power.

Shanghai Occupies a Position

The world's economic market is led by London in England, followed by New York in the United States. However, the US has repeatedly thought about absorbing the London market, seeing that England's policies and methods of concentrating commercial goods are excellent, but the US ultimately failed. But Shanghai once occupied the third position in the world economic market because goods can be sold in Shanghai. In the past, no matter what country's goods or what kind of goods, as long as they are slightly cheaper after arriving in Shanghai, there will definitely be buyers. Therefore, foreigners call Shanghai a dumping market. Now that the US has abandoned the gold standard, it can be said that it has no effect on the Shanghai market.

Air Force Defending Air Force

Airplanes are Better Than Anti-Aircraft Guns

Aviation Association Decides to Purchase First

Mr. Lin Wojang's Conversation

During the fourth report on aviation solicitation achievements, Wu Tiecheng, the solicitation team leader and mayor, proposed ordering twelve airplanes to form a squadron and go north to resist the enemy. However, the general opinion of the public is that it is better to deploy more anti-aircraft guns to defend against enemy planes, because the number of Chinese and Japanese air force planes is too far apart, and increasing one or two squadrons will probably not benefit the military much. A reporter from the New Voice News visited Mr. Lin Wojang, secretary-general of the Aviation Association, yesterday morning to inquire about the progress of ordering airplanes and whether air defense is beneficial. According to Mr. Lin, the association plans to purchase eighteen airplanes first, forming two squadrons. After the results of the Shanghai solicitation, the funds will be paid to order the airplanes, because the situation in North China is becoming increasingly dangerous, so there is a proposal to order the airplanes earlier. All directors expressed their agreement. The order will be placed after approval at next week's regular meeting. It has not yet been specifically decided which country and factory to order from. Foreign aviation and military experts believe that the effectiveness of airplanes is better than anti-aircraft guns for air defense. Because anti-aircraft guns are fixed in position, they can only be effective if enemy planes fly within their range. However, airplanes have a very high speed, and the opportunity to hit them is very small. Therefore, the most effective method is still to defend the air force with the air force.

After the Signing of the Temporary Telephone Contract

Public Works Bureau Director Xu's Remarks

Shanghai Telephone Company's Announcement

Director's Remarks

The Central News Agency reports that the temporary telephone contract signed by the Municipal Public Works Bureau, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, and the Shanghai Telephone Company was formally signed on the 19th of this month. The Guomin News Agency reports that the Shanghai Telephone Company in the Shanghai Concession issued a notice to the cross-boundary road users yesterday after signing a telephone contract with the Chinese municipal authorities for building roads beyond the boundaries. The notice stated that there would be many changes in the installation procedures and telephone rates. The contents are recorded as follows: "Regarding the telephone issue outside the two concessions, our company has obtained the consent of the Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession and the Public Works Bureau of the French Concession, and has signed a contract with the Municipal Public Works Bureau of the Shanghai Special Municipality and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications today (i.e., the day before yesterday). This contract is temporary in nature, and either party may cancel it by notifying the other party three months in advance. However, during the validity period of this temporary contract, both parties should still negotiate a permanent solution." 1. For those who installed telephones in the area beyond the western district road before January 1, 1932, an additional one yuan and four jiao per line per quarter must be paid as a royalty for the Shanghai Municipality's concession. This fee will be calculated from the next quarter's telephone bill and collected together. 2. Users who install telephones after January 1, 1932, must also sign a letter of guarantee and submit it to the Municipal Public Works Bureau for record, in addition to the above-mentioned measures. 3. For users who installed telephones outside the western district road area before November 20, 1932 (within one year), the company can pay 7.5 yuan per quarter to the Chinese-controlled telephone bureau on their behalf. 4. For those who installed telephones after November 20, 1932, the users must handle this fee themselves. Stores and residents in the Nanshi, Zhabei, and Pudong areas of the Chinese-controlled area who wish to install telephones in the concession can be accepted by the company; however, according to the contract, the Nanshi Telephone Bureau may notify the company to dismantle the telephone at any time, and the company shall not refuse. In such cases, the company will disconnect the line one month after receiving the notice, and the user shall not question the company. In addition to paying the telephone fee, they must also pay an additional one tael of silver and one yuan and four jiao. The telephone fees in the area beyond the road in the northern district are the most complicated, divided into (A) those whose houses are adjacent to the road and have at least one access to the road must pay 12 yuan per year to the Nanshi Telephone Bureau in addition to paying the company's telephone fees; (B) those whose houses are contrary to the situation in item A, that is, the houses are more than 100 yards away from the road, each user must pay an additional 60 yuan per year to the Nanshi Telephone Bureau; (C) in addition to the fees in items A and B, an additional 1.4 yuan must be paid as a royalty for the municipal concession; (D) if the concession taxpayer installed the telephone before November 20, 1932, the company can pay 7.5 yuan per quarter to the Nanshi Telephone Bureau within one year; (E) if it is not a concession taxpayer, the user shall bear this fee; (F) all users beyond the road in the northern district, whether new or old, must sign a letter of guarantee and submit it to the Municipal Public Works Bureau for record.

Shanghai Japanese Cotton Mills Implement Work Reduction

Average Reduction of 20% in Each Factory

Now Decided to Reduce to 40%

Recently, due to poor cotton yarn sales and extremely bad market conditions, Chinese cotton mills stopped working on Saturday and Sunday day and night shifts on the 22nd. According to the investigation, Japanese cotton mills in China have also long implemented work reductions. Currently, the Japanese factories in Shanghai that have reduced work are: Yufeng 10%, Rihua 30%, Shanghai Factory 10%, Nei Wai Cotton Yarn 15%, Gongda Factory 40%, Dakang Factory 10%, Tongxing Factory 5%, Donghua Factory 50%, and Toyota Factory 5%, with an average work reduction of about 20% in each factory. According to the Shanghai Japanese Daily News yesterday, the Nei Wai Cotton Yarn Factory has increased its stock of cotton yarn and cloth, and recently convened a meeting with various factories. As a result, it was decided to implement a 40% work reduction, and it is said that other factories will follow suit.

The procedures have been completed and urgently need to be transported. Women's Association Reports on the Northern Comfort Trip

Describing the Bravery of the Soldiers at the Front

Lamenting the Lack of a Comprehensive Government Plan

The Chinese Women's Association for Relief of Northeast Compatriots held a meeting of all initiators at its association on Fuxing Road on the 19th. Ms. Shen Huilian, Wang Xiaoying, and Wei Ying reported on their recent northern comfort trip, mainly stating that the purpose of their northern trip was to inspect the real war situation at the front, comfort the soldiers, wounded soldiers, and refugees, and to inspire the public and awaken compatriots to rise together and become the government's backing. Because its meaning was significant, they did not hesitate to endure hardships, travel long distances, not fearing enemy shells, not missing the elderly and young at home, and resolutely went north, departing on March 29 and arriving in Ping on April 3. They immediately visited Minister He and various agencies and organizations to discuss comfort procedures. The next day, they went to Xifengkou and met General Song Zheyuan, expressing their condolences and sending condolence funds. Then, they visited the battlefield, seeing that the defensive works were very solid, and the heroic spirit of the soldiers overflowed from their eyebrows. Everyone was determined to die for the country. The morale was high, which was admirable. They also saw the trophies such as Tangke vehicles, machine guns, steel helmets, military uniforms, and military flags. The enemy's new-era military fire was conquered by our old-era broadswords, which shows that the determination of morale is far better than sharp weapons. After sending condolence funds to the various fronts, they went to the rear hospitals to comfort the wounded soldiers and personally distributed condolence funds in front of the hospital beds. For the injured officers, they also sent flowers and fruits to comfort their spirits. All the injured officers and soldiers were thinking about the war situation at the front, and while moaning, they hoped that the wounds would heal quickly so that they could go to the front line to kill the enemy again. The seriously wounded had fractured limbs and rotting muscles, moaning intermittently. They felt sad and indignant about it. Therefore, compatriots who live in the rear should work hard to help these brave soldiers who are fighting for the country. It is estimated that in addition to the twelve rear hospitals in Beiping City, there are also hospitals in Tongzhou, Jixian, Zunhua, Kangzhuang, Zhangjiakou, and Shijiazhuang. They visited them in batches. They also visited the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese Return Group and sent a donation of 1,000 yuan. Minister He also visited and mentioned that since coming to Ping, he had set up supply stations, opened rear hospitals, built roads, and set up electric wires and telephones to facilitate military affairs. He also introduced them to visit the defensive works in the city, and they realized that the authorities were determined to resist. The total amount of condolence funds and goods was more than 27,000 yuan. They regretted that the various armies at the front lacked so much materials that they did not have enough money to help them. They deeply hoped that all circles would make efforts to help the soldiers fighting at the front. In short, the impressions after their northern comfort trip were that there were several points worth noting: 1. The morale of the various armies was very high, and they were all able to die for the country; 2. The supply of materials to the various armies was extremely lacking, and transportation was even more difficult; 3. Most of the people in northern China were superstitious and did not believe that the Japanese would invade Beiping and Tianjin. Therefore, when they were in Ping, they saw the masses coming and going in the spring sunshine, as if they had forgotten that the Japanese invaders were about to swallow them up; 4. They did not have a comprehensive plan, and they were afraid that the land would be lost piece by piece and never return.

The Self-Awareness of Nanjing Road Shops

Those Who Do Not Sell Inferior Goods Are Even More Determined

Those Who Mistakenly Sold Inferior Goods Repent

The Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens' Association, in order to encourage patriotism and promote the businessmen's fulfillment of their national salvation duties, have been actively inspecting the shops on Nanjing Road in the areas under the two associations for days to prevent the revival of inferior goods. The general situation has been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. It is now known that after the two associations officially announced the survey results in the newspapers on April 18, all the shops on the road unanimously strived to improve. Those who had already cleaned up and received the proof of merit card became even more determined. Those who had been cleaned up but were still under investigation by the two associations asked the associations to issue the proof of merit card as soon as possible to show their honesty and guarantee. In addition, the manager of the Tongchengcang Foreign Goods Store personally went to the association to explain that the inclusion of a small number of inferior goods in the past was not intentional, and made a written statement that all inferior goods had been cleaned up, requesting the association to send personnel to investigate again and grant the certificate, etc. The Xiexinxiang Store, which has already taken over the store of the Chinese shop, also sent a letter to the association stating that it had sealed up a small number of inferior goods that had been taken over and requested the association to send a commissioner to seal them up. The association, considering that the shops were brave in doing good, which shows that the national salvation work is still feasible, specially sent personnel to inspect again yesterday, and they were indeed cleaned up. The association immediately sealed them up, totaling 107 sections sealed up by Tongchengcang, divided into five display windows, and 43 sections sealed up by the Chinese store, divided into five packages. For Tongchengcang Store, the association agreed to issue a proof of merit card due to its membership relationship (the association does not provide proof to non-members for the time being), and it is also listed as one of the stores that do not sell inferior goods. It is also heard that the two associations will withdraw the proof of merit card if they find inferior goods in the stores that have already received the proof of merit card in the future.

Regulations on State-Run Trade with Russia

Concentrate Goods for Export to Russia

Exported in the Name of the State

The Central News Agency reports that the Regulations on State-Run Trade with Soviet Russia in our country have been drafted by He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, and submitted to the Ministry for approval, and then submitted to the Executive Yuan for review. The general idea of the regulations on state-run trade is to concentrate the national goods exported to Russia and export them in the name of the state. Part of the procedures adopts the Soviet Russian method of foreign trade. The detailed regulations will be announced after being approved by the Executive Yuan.

Four Batches of Antiquities Headed South Yesterday Morning

Storage Problem Resolved

Four batches of antiquities from the Palace Museum were shipped south yesterday under the supervision of Ma Heng, the director of the Palace Museum. According to sources from the local antiquities storage depot, the four batches of antiquities departed from Beijing at 8:00 AM yesterday and are expected to arrive in Pukou on the 23rd. The depot has already notified the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to send a ship to receive them. As for the storage location, due to the lack of suitable buildings, the depot staff yesterday reorganized the antiquities stored at the former site of the Catholic Renji Hospital, freeing up a space to store the four batches of antiquities, so no further search for buildings will be conducted.
