The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests the Imposition of Import Duties on Foreign Rice and Wheat

Levy Taxes on Foreign Goods

To Save Rural Bankruptcy

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industries, requesting the imposition of import duties on foreign rice and wheat to save the rural economy from bankruptcy. The original text reads: "Submitting a request based on the situation. On the 19th of this month, the Miscellaneous Grain Traders Guild stated in a letter: 'Our country has vast lands and abundant resources, and the grain produced is sufficient for self-sufficiency, so there is no need for foreign rice. Unfortunately, after the ravages of war, we have suffered severe floods, resulting in a continuous influx of foreign rice and wheat flour, with countless amounts of money flowing out of the country. Fortunately, last year's bumper harvest in the provinces along the Yangtze River allowed farmers and merchants to recover. Unexpectedly, due to global overproduction, rice, wheat, and flour have been rushing into our country, engaging in price-dumping competition without end, causing grain prices to plummet and farmers and merchants to suffer. Taking rice as an example, the farmers’ yield is insufficient to cover their expenses. Guild merchants transport goods from producing areas to Shanghai, but all suffer losses. Rice from Hunan and Jiangxi relies on purchases from Fujian to barely maintain a sales channel. However, supply exceeds demand, making it difficult to reverse the declining trend. Taking the current value in this city into account, top-grade machine-polished rice from Hunan and Jiangxi costs no more than 8.23 yuan per stone when transported from the origin to Shanghai. Various external expenses such as bags, water transport, and packaging require an additional 2.00 to 2.50 yuan per stone. Therefore, the selling price at the origin is only about 6 yuan. Converting rice from paddy rice to machine-polished rice results in about half of the paddy lost as bran and husks. Therefore, the farmers only receive 2.45 yuan for each stone of paddy. Low grain prices are harming farmers to the extreme. It is found that Guangdong and Guangxi are rice-deficient areas, with an annual shortage of about 10 million stones. In terms of supply, the surplus rice from Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang last year is sufficient to meet the demand. However, a detailed examination of rice purchases and sales in Guangdong and Guangxi reveals that only Wuhu ships a small amount, with foreign rice seizing the rest. Currently, the stock of foreign rice arriving in Shanghai is quite large, and the market price is as cheap as mentioned above. Moreover, the value of foreign rice is decreasing, and it is frequently heard that orders are still being placed in secret. If this continues, the disastrous decline in grain prices will be endless. As for wheat, domestically produced wheat will be available in two months. Even if flour mills need to order foreign wheat, it should be limited to meet the needs for two months. However, the reality is not so. Various types of foreign wheat from Australia, Canada, and Argentina are being eagerly ordered from abroad due to their low prices, and merchants are dumping their goods in the domestic market as much as possible. When domestic wheat is harvested, both farmers and merchants will suffer losses. Summing up the various points, it concerns the national economy and the people's livelihood. The Shandong provincial government has already passed a resolution to ban the import of foreign wheat flour and has submitted a request to the central government for implementation. With external troubles and internal worries, rural areas are on the verge of bankruptcy, and commercial transportation is on the verge of extinction. If import duties on foreign rice and wheat flour are not urgently imposed, allowing them to flood the market, then our country will not only perish from foreign aggression, but also from the bankruptcy of the rural economy. Therefore, we specially submit this request and appeal to be forwarded to the central government, ordering the Ministry of Finance to earnestly implement it in order to maintain agricultural production and alleviate the people's suffering. It is a great benefit.' The guild also stated that last year, the provinces in the Yangtze River basin all reported bumper harvests. Taking Hunan rice as an example, the provincial government proposed to transport and sell it directly to Guangdong Province. However, due to transportation costs, it was not as cost-effective as foreign rice, so it was discontinued. Jiangxi and Hunan provinces have not developed industry and mining, and have suffered heavily from banditry, greatly damaging their vitality. They rely entirely on the circulation of agricultural products for turnover. Therefore, the low-priced invasion of foreign rice requires taxation to provide some degree of control. Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have always relied on spring harvests to supplement autumn harvests. Last year's autumn harvest saw a sharp drop in rice prices, greatly impacting farmers. The silk industry has also been stagnant due to the sluggish sales of factory silk and low cocoon prices, with no sign of recovery. If wheat prices plummet again due to the dumping of foreign wheat, the livelihoods of farmers will be cut off, inevitably leading to them abandoning their fields. The weak will become starving corpses, and the cunning will take risks, which is a great danger to the heartland of the country. The guild's request to impose separate taxes is essential to save rural areas from bankruptcy. If this year’s harvest proves unstable, after the tax regulations are formulated, in the event of a poor harvest, when foreign rice and wheat are needed to supplement the supply, it is possible to temporarily exempt or reduce taxes within a specified period. This is a common practice in various countries and does not hinder the regulation of food supply. It is reasonable to submit this request to the Ministry for review and approval for implementation, as it is in the public interest."

The Executive Yuan Approves the Imposition of Land Value Tax in This City

Submit to the Municipal Government Meeting for Amended Draft Measures

According to Guomin News, the imposition of land value tax in this city has been planned and carried out by the preparatory committee organized by the Land and Finance Bureaus. The collection measures were submitted to the Municipal Government for forwarding to the Executive Yuan for review, with the intention of implementing them on July 1st of this year. It is now known that the Executive Yuan has approved the plan and sent it to Shanghai, including five proposed measures. However, due to three points that are quite inconvenient for implementation, the Land Bureau specially sent Yang Xiaotang, the head of the Second Section, to the Municipal Government yesterday to discuss the matter. It was decided that the measures proposed by the Executive Yuan would be submitted to the Municipal Government meeting this week for amendments. As for the scope of collection, it has been decided to implement it throughout the city, including the concessions.

Establishment of the Bicycle Repair and Rental Guild

Resolution to Suspend Business for Three Days to Assist Fellow Tradesmen in the French Concession

The Shanghai Bicycle Repair and Rental Guild held its inaugural meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Ningbo Native Place Association on Xizang Road. One hundred and eighty-three representatives from the industry throughout the city attended. Representatives from various agencies and organizations included Zhu Yaqui from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Song Zhongqing from the Social Bureau, Li Ruzhang from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tong Lizhang from the Fourth and Fifth Branches of the Second Special District of the Citizens' Association, and Tu Runcai and Wang Disheng from the Bicycle Manufacturing Guild. The details are recorded as follows.

Meeting Proceedings

After the meeting commenced, Han Baotai, Li Xiaoshi, Ji Hongnian, Li Fengting, and Xu Ruoyu were elected as the presidium. Formalities were observed. 1. Han Baotai reported on the preparations. 2. Li Xiaoshi reported on the income and expenditure during the preparatory period. 3. Ji Hongsheng reported on the illegal tax increases by the French Municipal Council, which forced fellow tradesmen to suspend business, and the process of requesting assistance from various agencies and public organizations. 4. Methods for assisting fellow tradesmen in the French Concession who were forced to suspend business were discussed. 8. The election of executive and supervisory committee members began. 9. The elected committee members took an oath of office. 10. A photograph was taken, refreshments were served, and the meeting adjourned. In the evening, a dinner was held for the elected committee members and representatives from all walks of life.

Assistance for Suspension of Business

Yesterday, all member tradesmen of the industry throughout the city discussed various methods of assisting fellow tradesmen in the French Concession who were forced to suspend business during the inaugural meeting. The first issue was whether to accept or reject the mediation of the French Concession Taxpayers' Association. It was resolved to accept the well-intentioned mediation on the one hand and continue the struggle on the other. As for how to proceed with the struggle, it was resolved: 1. To request the issuance of a declaration of assistance in the name of the inaugural meeting. 2. To request that all tradesmen in the city suspend business for three days to express sympathy. 3. To request that all tradesmen in the city hold a motorcade parade with banners reading "Assist French Concession Tradesmen in Suspending Business and Resisting Illegal Taxes" when necessary. 4. To request that the grievances of the tradesmen and the illegal tax increases by the French authorities be detailed and submitted to the relevant authorities for serious negotiations to abolish the harsh taxes in the name of the meeting. 5. To request that all trade guilds in the city be requested to assist and express sympathy in the name of the meeting. 6. To request that the meeting discuss various methods for fellow tradesmen in the French Concession to persistently resist the illegal and harsh taxes. 7. To request the establishment of a special committee to assist the suspension of business in the French Concession in the name of the meeting. 8. To request the dispatch of representatives to Beijing to petition when necessary. All the above methods were approved and handed over to the executive and supervisory committees for implementation.

Page 10

Nanyang Tobacco Factory Engineering Chief Li Hui Embezzles Bonus Money

Keeping the Bonus Money Without Distributing It

Over 130,000 Yuan Swallowed

The Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company's factory was once shut down due to poor business. After reorganization in the spring of 1931, work was resumed. In July of that year, the company's general manager convened a meeting with key factory personnel, including the chief and deputy foremen, the chief engineer, and the heads of various departments, and decided to switch to a contract labor system. A standard of 5,000 cases of cigarettes per month was set, with a production cost of 10 yuan per case. If the expenditure was insufficient, the company would still bear the burden. If there was a surplus, it would be used as a bonus for the workers, to be distributed equally among them. This system was purely intended to increase production and encourage workers. Since its implementation, it has been quite effective, with monthly surpluses in production costs. Therefore, Chief Engineer Li Hui was elected to be responsible for safekeeping and distributing the money on a regular basis. By the end of the year, after only a few months, each worker received a bonus equal to 72 days' wages. However, last year's overall production was even greater than in the past, but the bonus was not paid at all. Therefore, in mid-December of the lunar calendar, most of the workers inquired with their respective department heads and requested payment. The department heads then inquired with Li Hui, who said that the company had not paid the money. The workers then sent letters to the company's general manager, Jian Yujie, questioning him. Jian then convened a meeting and decided to hire accountant Xu Yongzuo to thoroughly audit the accounts. Unexpectedly, while Xu was auditing, Li Hui, knowing that there were untruths and omissions in the accounts, feared that once everything was found out, it would be unfavorable to him. He then colluded with a portion of the workers, including Zhang Desheng, and opposed the audit, claiming that the company should not interfere with the workers' accounts, and forcibly demanded the return of the account books. However, Jian had already taken photographs of the account books beforehand to keep as evidence. Although some of the negatives were also taken away, many still existed, as well as Xu's audit report, so it is still possible to understand the production quantity last year. From January to December, a total of 98,730 cases of cigarettes and 34,650 cigarettes were produced. The actual production cost paid out for the entire year was 771,486.16 yuan, averaging 7.81 yuan per case. According to the fixed quota of 10 yuan per case, there should be a surplus of 215,743.31 yuan, all of which was paid to Li Hui for safekeeping. However, Li only paid out worker bonuses twice in January of this year, totaling 73,486.10 yuan, leaving over 142,000 yuan still in storage. Recently, 10,000 yuan was donated to the Volunteer Army from this money. The actual stored amount of over 130,000 yuan is all in Li's hands. Currently, workers Feng Jialu, Wang Yuanding, Wang Ajin, Ying Jinbao, Wang Jincai, Zhang Bingkun, Wei Jinhua, Xin Rongda, Cai Guiqing, Kong Wanli, Wang Xuexiao, and others have repeatedly approached Li Hui, wanting to know the details of Li Hui's safekeeping and why the money was not immediately distributed, but all were unsuccessful. Therefore, they hired lawyer He Xianzhang to file a criminal lawsuit against Li Hui for embezzlement in the First Special District Court, stating that the defendant, as the person in charge of the bonus money, had such vague accounts, and dared to forcibly take away the account books and obstruct the audit afterwards, intending to embezzle the money. The plaintiffs' hard-earned money has been swallowed up, which is difficult to bear. They requested that the defendant be ordered to hand over the account books, verify the information, and be punished according to the law, and to order the payment of the remaining bonus money for fair distribution, to punish corruption and show justice. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Judge Wu Tingqi of the First Special District Court opened the court for trial. The defendant Li Hui avoided appearing in court. The plaintiffs all came to court with their lawyers and requested that since the defendant was avoiding appearing, a warrant should be issued so that the plaintiffs could apprehend him, so that their hard-earned money would not be lost. The Nanyang Company will also send its legal advisor, lawyer Wu Linkun, to court to listen to the trial. Judge Wu approved the plaintiffs' request and ordered that the case be adjourned to April 29 for further hearing.

Verdict in the Apprentice's Assault Case

Xie Moude Found to Have a Mental Disorder

Declared Not Guilty Yesterday

Xie Moude, a native of Nanjing, 19 years old, works as an apprentice at the Dongfang Trust Company at No. 323 Fujian Road. He is usually very amiable and helpful to others, and is quite diligent in his work, so his colleagues treat him with respect. However, at 2:00 AM on the 3rd of last month, while people were fast asleep, Xie suddenly took a kitchen knife and continuously injured four colleagues, Wang Ruixiu, Wang Wencheng, Gu Xuetong, and Xia Fengfei, before fleeing. After investigation by the police, Xie was apprehended at the Dahua Hotel. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, filed a public prosecution with the First Special District Court in accordance with Article 248 of the Criminal Code. Xie also hired a lawyer to defend him, claiming that Xie had a mental disorder. After the court sent Xie to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for examination, the results showed that Xie did have a mental disorder. After the conclusion of the debate, yesterday morning, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, Feng Shide, ascended to the Criminal Division One and declared Xie Moude not guilty. If the police do not appeal, his uncle, Qin Zhongying (the current county magistrate of Xiuning County), will take him back to be responsible for his medical treatment.

Two Kidnappers in Child Kidnapping Case Sentenced to Death

The home of Hu Henian, a Shaoxing native and runner for the World Bank at No. 493 Wayside Road, was broken into by bandits in the late hours of February 24th of this year. Valuables worth over 40 yuan were stolen, and as they fled, they kidnapped Hu's two-year-old son, Guoan, and demanded a large ransom. Subsequently, Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Inspectorate, along with Inspectors Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, Shao Jingfan, and others, arrested the kidnappers Wang Weisheng, Zhang Songyao, Sun Zhiming, Zhu Zhonggeng (also known as Genglong), Liu Qin, Yu Jisheng, and the women Jin Xiaomei, Wu Zhou, Wu Yuchun, and Ma Afeng, totaling ten people. A Mauser pistol and 212 bullets were seized, and Hu Guoan was rescued in Macan Village, Ningbo. Sadly, he died of illness within six days, which is regrettable. The First Special District Court, which accepted the case, has concluded its interrogation. Yesterday afternoon, presiding judge of the Criminal Division, Qian Hongye, opened the court to announce the verdict. The police prosecutor, lawyer Ru Baoyi, was also present to await instructions. Qian then announced that Zhu Zhonggeng and Yu Jisheng were sentenced to death, Wang Weisheng was sentenced to life imprisonment, Liu Qin and Ma Afeng were sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment each, Zhang Songyao was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment, and Sun Zhiming, Jin Xiaomei, Wu Zhou, and Wu Yuchun were all found not guilty. The Mauser pistol and 212 bullets were confiscated.

The Municipal General Labor Union Advocates for Rickshaw Pullers

French Police Arbitrarily Take Photos and Impose Fines

Requesting the Taxpayers' Association to Negotiate

The Municipal General Labor Union sent a letter to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, according to the representatives of rickshaw pullers, Zhang Asi, Wang Deda, Jin Are, Zhu Lusi, and others, the French police have been dispatching officers every night to take photos of permits regardless of whether the rickshaw pullers are at fault, and a fine of 50 cents is required the next day to retrieve the permit. Our rickshaw pullers earn only a few cents for running around every day. If they are unexpectedly fined, their livelihood for the day is not guaranteed. Now, the French Concession constables disregard humanitarianism and arbitrarily impose fines, causing unbearable harm to the workers. Therefore, we find it after investigation, everyone knows the suffering of rickshaw pullers, and they are all ignorant people. Even if there is a slight fault, they should be treated leniently due to their ignorance. However, the French police now take photos and impose fines regardless of whether there is a violation, which is very inappropriate if true. Therefore, we specially request your association to seriously negotiate with the French authorities to immediately stop the illegal photography in order to maintain humanitarianism and sympathize with the hardships of the workers. Sincerely, this is for the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association."

The Health Bureau Advances the Date of Vaccination

Sends letters to the Education and Social Bureaus for assistance

The Municipal Health Bureau sent letters to the Education and Social Bureaus stating: "We are writing to inform you that cholera is known to be a serious disease, and the results of our bureau's preventive vaccination have been proven to be effective over the years. As summer is approaching, our bureau has prepared for this prevention plan and intends to start implementation from May 1st. All teachers and students in the city's schools (factory employees and workers) will be vaccinated before the summer vacation (in advance). In addition to the vaccination dates being scheduled by our bureau and directly notified to each school (factory), we are concerned that the schools (factories) may not understand the principle and be unwilling to accept it. Therefore, we are writing to request your bureau to instruct all schools (factories) to accept cholera preventive vaccination to jointly maintain health. We are sending this letter accordingly, hoping that you will investigate and handle it appropriately, and extend our public friendship."

Sanitary Conditions in the Public Concession in March

The Municipal Council's Health Officer's report for March stated: "The death rate for foreigners this month was 15.45, compared to 14.21 last month. The death rate for Chinese was 13.06, compared to 16.99 last month. The total number of Chinese deaths reported was 1,149, 340 less than last month. This is probably because fewer abandoned corpses were found.

The birth statistics show that 60 reports were received for foreigners and 104 for Chinese, as well as 37 births of non-residents. The collection of these statistics is now being improved.

This month, 41,296 people were vaccinated against smallpox, mostly through mobile vaccination units, and mostly through health sub-bureaus. The total number is four times higher than in February, due to many vaccinations being given during the Flower Birthday. Furthermore, the effect of posting slogans in various places and publicizing in vegetable markets and other public places has been quite effective.

Among foreigners, the most common infectious diseases were scarlet fever and tuberculosis. Among Chinese, they were cerebrospinal meningitis, tuberculosis, and typhoid fever. Smallpox was also reported slightly, and the rest were less common. The momentum of scarlet fever has also decreased. The actual number of influenza cases is probably higher than reported, as influenza often leads to pneumonia, and pneumonia is quite common.

Cerebrospinal meningitis has increased significantly among Chinese (but foreigners have not been affected). This increase is late in the season and is unlikely to develop significantly. However, this disease seems to have taken root in Shanghai. Once it enters a crowded area, death from this disease is inevitable. The only solution is to wait for the expansion of the city, with more open space, roads, and parks to reduce population density and change living conditions. As for preventive medicine in the current state, it is not easy to quickly eradicate the disease.

The pathological research laboratory tested 1,469 cases this month. Sixty-one people sought treatment for rabies, including five from other places. Forty-three of them were ordered to undergo treatment.

Due to several warm days this month, mosquitoes appeared early. Oiling work in various places began immediately. There have also been many public reports of wind patients. 3,300 wind patients have been caught in the central and northern districts. Several smaller houses in various places were ordered to be whitewashed, and several were prosecuted. In one area, there were 900 inspections and 400 warnings were issued."

The Chinese Ratepayers Association Sends a Letter to the Municipal Council

Requests that the maintenance of public health should not harm the legitimate rights of citizens

The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "According to Mr. Feng Guochang's letter, he recently received a letter from the Chief of the Health Department of the Municipal Council on April 3rd, stating, 'It has been found that the Chinese restaurant at 698 Avenue Edward VII has unsanitary conditions, such as 1. Dirty and dilapidated floors, walls, and ceilings, 2. Unclean and damaged refrigerators, 3. Using natural ice, 4. Insufficient fuel storage space, 5. Unauthorized construction in the back, 6. Accumulated garbage. You should inform your shopkeeper in detail and ask them to clean up the areas pointed out by this bureau. If you want to know the details, please inquire at the medical officer's office between 10:00 AM and 12:00 PM every day.' After receiving the letter, our office immediately followed it on the 13th and commissioned Mr. Shao Yijian to go to the bureau to meet the Chief of the Health Department in order to appeal in person. At that time, a secretary met on his behalf. After inquiring about the situation, he wrote a note and asked to contact the garbage officer. After seeing the note, the garbage officer introduced him to another Westerner, who commissioned a Chinese Mr. Wang to inquire about the process. Our office stated our intention and defended each point. However, Mr. Wang said that there was nothing difficult to do in these points, and after following the instructions, one could go to the Health Sub-Bureau at the corner of Guangxi Road, Sima Road, to request a re-examination and it would be over. Because there was no responsible person in charge, we could not accept the defense and wasted time, so we left. According to the first, second, and sixth points in the bureau's letter, our office repairs and cleans them regularly, and even if the bureau does not come to inspect, we always pay attention to handling them, so there is no need to discuss these points. Regarding the third point about using natural ice, Article 16 of the bureau's food license states, 'Any cooked or raw food should not be in contact with natural ice.' The items stored in the refrigerator are all uncooked, which is consistent with the license. Moreover, the principle of using ice is to prevent food from spoiling. The bureau should ask whether the principle is the same, so why distinguish between natural ice and artificial ice? Regarding the fourth point, the fuel storage space is insufficient. Our office purchases fuel every day, so no matter what, the storage space should be sufficient. Regarding the fifth point, there is unauthorized construction in the back. Our office only put up a shed in the patio to block the wind and rain, which should not be unsanitary. If it is said that it is unauthorized, there are countless unauthorized buildings in this city. How can the Health Department inspect and order them to be demolished one by one? In short, our office respects the bureau's regulations and does not offer any unspoken rules, which has caused resentment, so it is deliberately trying to add to our guilt. In this time of economic hardship, maintaining operations is already insufficient. If we want to destroy it again, the future hidden worries are unbearable to imagine. It is reported that the Shanghai Municipal Council's budget is short by 1.5 million this year, so it intends to increase the municipal general tax. If the Municipal Council's budget is insufficient, it is natural to think of increasing it on the citizens. However, can we merchants say that expenses are insufficient and increase the selling price? It should be known that no one cares about reducing the actual price. Your association is the mouthpiece of the taxpayers in this city. Therefore, we have reported the details one by one and ask you to inform the bureau so that the bureau does not stand on the position of the Municipal Council of material civilization to face the citizens, but should love the citizens with the intention of understanding the merchants' difficulties. Otherwise, in fact, due to social and economic relations, the citizens are unlikely to satisfy the bureau.' After investigating the matter, we believe that attaching importance to public health is a necessary action in municipal administration. However, if it exceeds the scope of possible implementation, or is close to being demanding, or even has the reason for the attacks in the letter, and is overly critical, it should be stopped to prevent harming the legitimate rights of citizens while maintaining public health. Based on the above, we are sending this letter to your bureau, hoping that you will give it serious consideration. This is addressed to the Director-General of the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council."

Recent News from the Jiangsu Province Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association

The Tobacco and Alcohol Industry in Wuxi Details its Suffering

The tobacco and alcohol industries in various counties of Jiangsu Province, in view of the increasing fees and taxes over the years that have become unbearable, have been contacting each other and organizing a provincial tobacco and alcohol industry association to work together, unite, and seek liberation. Since the nine trade associations in the city, including the tobacco exchange industry, have been responsible for preparations, it has been a little over ten days and they have already received letters and telegrams of support from trade associations in various counties. Many have joined, and the situation has been reported in previous newspapers. Now, according to a letter from the two industries in Wuxi detailing the suffering of fees and taxes, it is specially recorded as follows. The Tobacco Exchange and Cigarette Trade Associations wrote: "In reply, we have respectfully noted the contents of your letter. It is found that the government regards this tax as a profit. Over the years, the ratio has increased, and merchants have not been spared. Since the 19th year of the Republic of China, the competent authorities have repeatedly called for the relief of merchants, but in reality, every time the general and sub-bureaus change, the tobacco and alcohol merchants increase their burden once, and the changes become more and more severe, squeezing the marrow, making the tobacco and alcohol merchants suffer the pain of being unable to survive. Your association sees the crux of the problem and has launched a provincial tobacco and alcohol merchant association in order to unite and work together to seek legitimate ways to reduce the burden on merchants. This is indeed an essential plan. Our associations followed the instructions and convened a joint meeting. Everyone believed that the matter was closely related to their own interests and dared not hesitate. It has been decided to reply to your association to express our sympathy and ask you to convene a general meeting as soon as possible. We are sending this letter accordingly, hoping that you will investigate and handle it appropriately." The Liquor, Medicine, and Store Trade Association wrote: "The tobacco and alcohol industry has suffered from the frequent increases in tax rates over the years, resulting in sluggish business. Our local industry has felt unbearable pain. In recent years, it has been difficult for merchants in both industries to maintain their operations. Therefore, many have stopped their businesses. If we do not work together to remedy the situation and relieve the pain, the burden will inevitably become heavier in the future. Now, we have read in the newspaper that your association has launched preparations to organize the Jiangsu Provincial Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association and has sent letters to the tobacco and alcohol trade associations in various counties to solicit opinions. After investigating, the annual tax collection period for this year is approaching. Our local industry is planning to discuss remedial measures. We have learned of your association's proposal and express our deep approval. Since you have taken the lead, our association should humbly follow in your footsteps. Please take charge of everything and actively proceed, and we hope that you will give us instructions at any time so that we can follow them. This is our sincere prayer. We are sending this letter specifically, hoping that you will investigate and handle it appropriately."

Recognition for Inspector Shen's Retirement

Shen Defu, Detective Inspector of the French Concession Police Department, has served in the French Municipal Council for 33 years. He is diligent and has been praised by his superiors. From 1907 to 1912, most of the important assassination and theft cases in the French Concession were solved by Mr. Shen. He has received the First Class Baoguang Medal from the government (1920), a medal from the Governor-General of Annam (1924), and a gold medal from the French Municipal Council (1927). Over the years, he has been relied upon by the French Concession authorities. Now, Mr. Shen is approaching seventy years old and his physical strength is not sufficient. He has applied for retirement to recuperate. The French Consul-General in Shanghai believes that Mr. Shen has served the Labor Bureau for 30 years as if it were one day and has achieved remarkable results. Now that he is old and retiring, it is not enough to encourage him without giving him special recognition. He has been generously awarded a bonus and a certificate as a permanent memento.

Business and Academic Circles Pay Attention to the Iron Exhibition

Since the opening of the Railway Goods Exhibition, most of the visitors have been from the business and academic circles. It is said that business people who attend the exhibition must purchase the association's publications on railway transportation regulations. The association has sold more than 5,000 copies of this publication. The academic community often copies the association's statistical charts and graphs, which shows that the business and academic communities in Shanghai are paying attention to the Iron Exhibition.

New Detention Center at the Zhanghuabang Customs

The Shanghai Customs and River Affairs Department recently built a detention center next to the Chinese office in the Zhanghuabang Customs. The construction has been completed. It is said that in the future, anyone found smuggling prohibited items on ships, or any shipowner who stops and throws goods on the road in violation of the route, will be detained. Because the original personnel in the Zhanghuabang Customs are insufficient to dispatch, a Westerner and several Chinese staff members have been transferred from the Shanghai Customs Yangshupu River Patrol Boat to Songjiang to serve. It is expected that it will be implemented on May 1st.

Robbery of a Women's Incense Burning Group

Roaming in Hangzhou and Jiaxing, Berthing in Zhapu at Midnight

Bandits Search and Rob, Returning Empty-Handed to Shanghai

The wife of Zheng Xiangru, who lives in Zhabei and is in the foreign goods business, recently gathered her girlfriends to burn incense in Hangzhou. She hired Yang Er, a Wuxi fast boat, and set off from Shanghai on the 12th of this month. There were more than ten people in the party, all women, and several maids. They arrived in Hangzhou on the 16th and finished burning incense. They asked Yang's boat to go to Jiaxing to visit the Misty Rain Tower and other famous scenic spots for a day. On the way back on the 18th, they passed through various towns and stopped to play. They sailed to Zhapu and it was dark. Mrs. Zheng asked Yang's boat to dock overnight and return to Shanghai the next day. Yang's boat docked. Suddenly, in the middle of the night, three or four small boats came, with two or three bandits in each boat. They rushed onto the boat, shone electric torches into the cabin, and the women, who were mostly asleep, woke up in shock upon hearing the noise and screamed. The bandits took out guns to threaten them and prevent them from making noise. The bandits searched everywhere and opened the boxes that everyone had brought. All the silver dollars were robbed, and the female passengers were forced to take off their rings and bracelets. The female passengers were frightened and stunned. After searching, they also searched Yang's boat and robbed Yang of sixty or seventy yuan and a leather suitcase. Before leaving, they fired a shot into the sky, and the bandits boarded the pirate ships and fled west. Mrs. Zheng and the other women were robbed of silver dollars and jewelry worth about a thousand yuan. One of the women was robbed of the most valuable items and injured her left hand. Yesterday, Yang's boat arrived in Shanghai, and the women returned home disappointed, complaining that the gods did not protect them.

Case of Fraud at Xiangxing Solved

Thirty-Nine Cases of Raw Oil

Xiangxing North Goods Store, located at No. 1 Tongan Lane, New Pier Street, Nanshi, this port, is opened by Wang Zhengxiang from Haizhou. It has been in business for many years and its business is considered to be quite developed. On the 11th of this month, a broker claiming to be surnamed Gu went to the store to buy thirty-nine cases of raw oil, the value of which was stated to be $213.75. The said Gu then hired a small cart to load the goods and instructed the store owner, Wang Zhengxiang, to follow him to No. 70 Xiangfen Lane, Nanjing Road, Public Concession to collect the money. Thereupon, Wang took a car and followed Gu to the place. Unexpectedly, Gu entered through the front door and escaped through the back door without a trace. Wang, having waited for a long time without seeing Gu pay the money, became suspicious. He then inquired at the house, but all replied that they did not know. Only then did he realize that he had been deceived. He immediately turned around and returned to the store to report, and suspected that the raw oil was loaded by the cart driver Yin Xiaokun, fearing that he might be in collusion with the fraud. He immediately reported the above to the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting investigation and arrest. After receiving the report, Captain Lu immediately ordered the Detective Team leader Wu Kezhong, detectives Dai Hongzhang, Chen Sirong, etc. to investigate separately. Later, the cart driver Yin Xiaokun was arrested at No. 12 Xiaocai Market, Zhonghua Xin Road, Zhabei, and the buyers of the stolen goods Feng Baosheng, Shen Xinting, and Rong Ruiting were arrested separately in the Chinese Concession. Twenty-one cases of the original stolen raw oil and two empty cases were recovered. They were escorted to the police station and transferred to the Detective Team for detention and interrogation.

Jiang Xiangrong Crushed to Death by Belt

Jiang Xiangrong, a Shaoxing native residing in Chongxin Workshop, Xiaoshadu, 47 years old, had been working as a laborer in the Dachang oil pressing machine room. On April 10, while working, his clothes were caught in the belt, and his body fell into the belt's rotating shaft, crushing his head and chest. He was immediately rescued by workers, but he was already unconscious. He was immediately taken to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was too late. He died of his injuries yesterday morning. His wife, Jiang Zhou, carried the body back to be coffined. The incident was learned by the police station, which immediately ordered Xu Chuliang, the local security officer of the Twelfth District of the South, to report to the Local Court for examination. The deceased's wife also filed a case requesting exemption from examination.

A piece of land at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue du Pères, covering nearly five acres, has now been purchased by the International Savings Society. It is reported that the price is approximately one million taels.

Xia Guisheng Arrested for Adultery and Abduction of Widow

Three Men and Women Detained in Suzhou

Shen Chen, a widow from Nanjing, 45 years old, runs Shen Yongxing Redwood Workshop at No. 58 Lingji Street, Yuxing Bridge, Dadongmen, Nanshi. The business is doing well and she has some savings. However, her husband and son have died one after another. In addition to her younger son Sanbao, her widowed daughter-in-law Shen Wu (23 years old), and grandson Guilin (6 years old), she also has an adopted daughter, 19 years old. The household expenses depend entirely on the redwood workshop and rent. However, Shen Wu is quite attractive. Shen Chen, considering that she is young and a widow, and that although she has a child, she may not be able to maintain her chastity, provides her with food and a monthly allowance of twenty yuan. Unexpectedly, Shen Wu is not accustomed to widowhood and often takes Guilin to play in the Xiaoshijie in the city, where she was seduced by Xia Guisheng from Suzhou who sings Tanhuang. Shen Wu, being young and inexperienced, was eventually tempted into adultery. She became intimate with Xia and they have been together for three years. At that time, Shen Chen noticed it, but because of her reputation, she did not make it public. Unexpectedly, Xia Guisheng became more and more brazen, and on the 13th of this month, he instigated Shen Wu to take the child Guilin, and steal gold jewelry including a gold bracelet, a gold hair clasp, five gold rings, a pair of gold earrings, a string of pearls, two inlaid rings, a black sheepskin robe and other clothes in a large package, as well as copper and tin utensils and other sundry items, and eloped without a trace. On the same day, the railway police of the Two-Way Management Bureau of the North Railway Station suspected their behavior and detained Xia Guisheng, Shen Wu, and Guilin for one night. Because there was no plaintiff to pursue the matter, they were released. Later, Shen Chen reported Shen Wu's elopement to the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting investigation. Detectives Xie Wanlin and Xu Zhaochang of the team learned that the railway police had intercepted and released them and that they had taken a train to Suzhou. The detectives went to Suzhou the day before yesterday and, together with detectives from the Suzhou Public Security Bureau, arrested the abductor Xia Guisheng, Shen Wu, and the child Guilin at Zhang Taihe Firecracker Shop, No. 49 Nianzhu Street, Xumen, and brought them back to the team. During interrogation, the abductor Xia Guisheng confessed that he was from Suzhou, residing at No. 12 Linde Lane, Fangbang Road, Shanghai, and made a living by singing Tanhuang at Xiaoshijie. He admitted that he had arrived in Suzhou on the 14th and confessed to seduction and abduction. When questioned, Shen Wu's confession was the same. After verifying the confessions, the captain of the team detained them and transferred them for further investigation.

Gangsters "Pai San He Tu"

A Hawker Faints

The areas of Ningbo Road and Rue Minitié and Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession are gathering places for hawkers. It is common for unemployed gangsters to extort cigarette money from the hawkers, resulting in fights and brawls. Yesterday at 1:00 PM, a similar incident occurred in front of the Ruixing Lane entrance opposite the Sino-French School. A hawker was subjected to "Pai San He Tu" (grabbing limbs and slamming them forcefully on the road) by five or six gangsters in the middle of the road, causing him to faint. The gangsters, seeing the trouble they had caused, tried to flee in a panic. Fortunately, a patrolman happened to pass by and caught the leader. He also tried to revive the hawker who had fainted. Then, he hired a car to take the injured person and the assailant to the Avenue Joffre Police Station to report to the head of the police for investigation.

Wu Runmin Detained for Fraud

Defrauding Money in the Name of Appealing on Behalf of Others

Yang Yi, a woman from Jiangbei, whose husband, Cunfu, was sentenced to death by the First Special District Local Court for robbery and other cases, was running around to rescue him. Through Zhou Xinquan, she met Wu Runmin, a man from Jiangbei, who claimed that he could handle the appeal. On March 14, she went to Wu's house with Zhou. There was a sign for the Twelfth Law Office of Jinzhi at the entrance, and Wu's business card stated that he was the director of the office. He ordered her to pay $5 first to prepare a petition and told her to go and check the approval herself. The woman searched everywhere at the notice board in front of the court, but could not find any approval. The next day, Wu copied out an approved instruction, saying that it was copied from the clerk's office because they were classmates, so it was convenient. He then ordered her to pay a public fee of $40. The woman paid $20 first, and Wu issued a receipt. Unexpectedly, on April 11, the defendants in the same case were all tried in court, but Yang Yi's husband was not mentioned, indicating that no appeal had been filed. Zhou and the woman demanded the money back from Wu. Unexpectedly, Wu went to the Nanshi Local Court to accuse Zhou and the woman of extortion and fraud. Yesterday, Judge Kong summoned Zhou and the woman for questioning. Zhou and the woman recounted the previous events and presented evidence. The judge believed that Wu himself had committed fraud, so he detained Wu and waited for the lawyer to come to the court for questioning.

Preface to the Shen Bao Yearbook

By Zhang Zisheng

"It is a scholar's shame to be ignorant of anything." This is an ancient saying.

"Scholars do not go out, yet they know the affairs of the world." In the past, knowledge was the exclusive property of the scholar-official class, and only scholars could "know the affairs of the world." However, in our era, it is different. Knowledge has become a necessity of life for the masses. A good citizen in the modern era must understand the common sense of politics, law, economics, society, and military affairs, and must understand the general trend of the country and the world. Whether it is a farmer, a businessman, a worker, or a student, a producer or a consumer, if they do not have a considerable understanding of all modern activities, even personal life will feel many difficulties, let alone serve the country and society.

The aspects of modern human activities are very broad and interconnected. Modern human production has changed from self-sufficient rural production to social production and national production. Professor of the Tokyo National Academy of Music, with many years of experience and profound artistry, occupies an important position in the modern music world. Four years ago, he toured the world with the world-renowned violinist Ms. Hanson, giving many concerts, which were very popular among the public. When he passed through Shanghai, Xiao Youmei, the president of the Shanghai Conservatory of Music, was shocked by his reputation and sincerely recruited him to be the director of the piano group. He has a large number of talented students, such as Li Xianmin and Jiu Fusheng, who will graduate this summer. It is heard that in addition to a public banquet to celebrate, the colleagues of the school will also give gifts as a souvenir.

Broadcasting Stations

Tianyi Company Self-Operated Radio Station Tianyi Film Company previously jointly operated a radio station with the China Radio Research Society. The machine part was handled by China, while Tianyi was responsible for the programs. It officially started broadcasting on February 1st and lasted for two months, with good results. However, the frequency of the station was 1140, which often interfered with other stations, resulting in unclear sound, which was a pity for the listeners. Now the company has rebuilt it on its own, named Tianyi Broadcasting Radio Station, with the equipment installed by the Asia Electric Company. The power is greater than before. It is currently preparing and has applied to the International Telecommunications Bureau for a test license, specifying the wavelength, frequency, and call sign. As soon as the preparations are completed, broadcasting can begin.

Youlian Broadcasting Station Adds Programs From today (21st), from 12:30 PM to 1:30 PM every afternoon, the Zhenhua Paint Company will rent the Youlian Company Broadcasting Radio Station at No. 419 Avenue Joffre and hire the famous storyteller Chen Lianqing and Qi Lianfang to sing and perform the book "Xiao Jin Qian". The station's radio wave is 880 kilocycles.

Radio Broadcasts Christian Lectures The International Bible Research Association has been broadcasting on the Zhongxi Broadcasting Station X CD every Sunday afternoon from 2:30 PM to 3:00 PM for seven times. It is heard that starting this Sunday, all the topics have been set: One, the Kingdom of God; Two, the End of the World; Three, the Battle of Armageddon; Four, the Transformation of the World. These five topics have a thorough and rational explanation of the causes of the current panic. The lectures are in English and translated by Mr. Chen Shiyan.

Letter

To the editor-in-chief of Shen Bao,

Sir,

Respectfully, I have read the section on local news in your newspaper on the 18th, which states that a treacherous merchant was caught smuggling Japanese fish, which is completely inconsistent with the facts. Now, I will tell you the true situation: At 3:00 AM on the 17th of this month, the Jinbaoli fishing boat entered the port and offered to sell to our firm. Because the customer was unfamiliar, our firm found the situation suspicious. When asked about the origin, the customer suddenly avoided meeting. Our firm reported to the water patrol police station and the customs. The customs sent personnel to monitor the action. However, the report in your newspaper is completely contrary to the facts. I am afraid that it will be misleading, so I am telling you the truth and hope that you will correct it in the letter column.

Sincerely,

Qiafeng Fish Bank

After discussions of dozens of colleagues, the editor-in-chief, editors, and special writers, reached thirty-one people, and with the cooperation of people from all walks of life, we were able to meet the people of the country. We feel that it is even more memorable: the first publication of the Shen Bao Yearbook coincides with the day of deep national crisis. The country and the nation are enduring humiliation and bearing heavy burdens, preparing their weapons and sharpening their swords in order to resist foreign aggression. Naturally, the Chinese nation has only one way out: to fight bravely, resist Japan, and oppose imperialism. However, with the complexity of modern national organizations, politics, economy, and culture are closely related to national defense. Moreover, the domestic situation and the international situation are intertwined and inseparable. If the entire nation does not have a deep understanding of the internal and external situations, it will not be able to resist foreign aggression and eliminate national disasters by relying solely on courage. Mr. Sun Yat-sen had the legacy of knowing is difficult but doing is easy. Ignorance is the nation's greatest weakness. The publication of the Shen Bao Yearbook is the greatest expectation of the colleagues if it can be of some service to the work of resisting Japan and opposing imperialism by increasing national awareness!

Finally, we should thank all parties for their support and hope that all enthusiastic and caring gentlemen will point out our shortcomings!

March 24, 1933.

Education News

Important News

The Central Political Conference Decides that Wang Shijie Will Be the Minister of Education

(Nanjing, 20th) The interim Central Political Conference held after the Standing Committee meeting resolved to appoint Wang Shijie, the president of Wuhan University, as the Minister of Education. The vacancy of the president will be filled by Tong Gengsheng, the director of the Department of Political Science of the university.

The Ministry of Education Orders that Libraries of Schools in Tianjin and Beijing Should Be Relocated

(Beiping, 20th) The Ministry of Education instructed that the libraries of schools in Tianjin and Beijing should be relocated. Currently, only Peking University is relocating first.

Reform of the School System in Southwest China

The Ministry of Education Submitted to the Executive Yuan Requesting that it Not Be Implemented, Which Has Been Approved

(Nanjing, 20th) The Ministry of Education stated that the Southwest Political Committee's decision to reform the school system, abolish winter and summer vacations, the length of study in schools at all levels, stipulated that primary and secondary schools each have five years and universities three to five years, and that it would hinder students' physical and mental rest and learning adjustment. Moreover, shortening the length of study would not only make it difficult to maintain the existing level of content in each subject, but also require a complete change in the allocation of teaching materials for each subject, and it is difficult to determine whether it can be implemented without hindrance. According to convention, students enter school at the age of six and graduate from primary school at the age of ten. Students graduate from secondary school at the age of sixteen. Generally, students lack a personal understanding of the subjects they study, whether they are natural or social sciences. Graduation from university is at the age of nineteen, which is still lower than the legal adult age of twenty, and they feel that they lack experience, which is contrary to common sense. Moreover, the national school system was originally unified. If some provinces suddenly act differently, it will not only disrupt the school system, but also make it difficult to transfer students to schools and for graduates to obtain qualifications and appointments. The Ministry of Education ordered the Guangdong Education Department not to implement it, and prepared opinions to be submitted to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Guangdong Provincial Government for non-implementation. It is heard that the Yuan's order was approved on the 20th.

The Ministry of Education Plans to Improve Primary Schools Across the Country

Adding Junior Primary Schools to Independent Senior Primary Schools

Establishing Research Associations Across the Board

(Nanjing, 20th) The Ministry of Education plans to rectify and improve primary schools across the country with six measures: Independent senior primary schools should all add junior primary schools, non-experimental primary schools should change their names, and primary schools should all establish research associations, etc. The Ministry issued orders to the education departments of all provinces and cities on the 20th to comply.

The Ministry of Education Issues a Circular to All Provinces and Cities to Strictly Hold Entrance Examinations

Refuting the Request of Private Schools in Beijing to Change the Entrance Examination Method

(Nanjing, 20th) The Ministry of Education stated that the level of graduates from public and private primary and secondary schools in all provinces and cities is highly inconsistent. Although most schools are able to strictly hold entrance and grade placement examinations, they are often not very serious about teaching, which is not a trivial matter that misleads students, and the society and the country are harmed as a result. On the 20th, the Ministry specially issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces and cities to strictly follow the temporary regulations on entrance examinations and the repeated orders, and to strictly hold entrance examinations without being negligent, so as to attach importance to education.

(Nanjing, 20th) The presidents of private secondary schools in Beijing previously jointly submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to instruct the Social Bureau to revise the entrance examination method. The Ministry of Education stated that the entrance examination for primary and secondary school graduates is to encourage educational progress and has repeatedly issued orders to strictly hold it. The several revised entrance examination methods proposed by the presidents of private secondary schools in Beijing either do not match the facts or contradict laws and regulations. In addition to detailed explanations, they were severely refuted and ordered to comply.

Local News

French Authorities Force Private Schools to Suspend Classes

School Principals Petition the Municipal Government

Requesting Serious Negotiations with the French Municipal Council

(Dagong News) The French Municipal Council has recently successively forced private schools in the concession to suspend classes without announcing the reasons. The principals of the schools believe that this move by the French authorities is clearly to destroy our country's education, and they have jointly petitioned the municipal government and the municipal education bureau to negotiate with the French authorities to immediately resume classes so as to prevent thousands of children in the concession from wasting their time and losing their education. In addition to sending personnel to investigate the truth, the Municipal Education Bureau has submitted a request to the government for instructions. At 2:00 PM yesterday, Chen Yingxian, the principal of the Leyuan Elementary School, and others went to the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Government to request negotiations for the resumption of classes. They first went to the Municipal Education Bureau, where they were received by Tang Jingxiu, an inspector of the bureau, who agreed to immediately investigate the truth of the French Municipal Council's order to suspend classes and then submit a request to the Municipal Government to negotiate with the French authorities. Then, they went to the Municipal Government, where they were received by Secretary Geng. The representatives stated that more than a dozen primary and secondary schools in the French Concession have been suspended in recent days without any reasons being announced. If the school facilities are inadequate or the management is poor, the French Municipal Council may send personnel to thoroughly investigate together with the Municipal Education Bureau. Unexpectedly, the French Municipal Council notified the schools on the 11th of this month and ordered them to suspend classes on the 13th. The schools are concerned that the long-term absence from classes will endanger the children's education, so they requested Secretary Geng to forward a request to the mayor to consult with the French authorities to resume classes first, and then discuss the negotiations. Secretary Geng agreed to call the Municipal Education Bureau to inquire about the investigation and then negotiate with the French authorities. If it is a local problem, it will be easy to solve. If it is a strategy of the French authorities, the Municipal Government must submit a request to the central government to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to seriously negotiate with the French side.

Municipal Health Education Exhibition

Scheduled for June 1st to 3rd

Exhibits Divided into School, Society, and Reference Groups

The preparatory committee for the Municipal Health Education Exhibition held its first meeting yesterday at the Municipal Education Bureau. The attending committee members included Wu Liguo, Sun Jiazhai, and Su Jielang from the Health Bureau; Zhou Feicheng, Chen Bai, Zhou Shang, Zhang Yongchun, Lu Bingqian, Hu Changcai, Wang Keyong, Yang Zhi, and Shen Yuguang from the Education Bureau; Cheng Kuan from Wusong Junior High School; and representatives from the China-Germany Midwifery School, Mao Zhongying; the Children's Morning Post, Zhao Zengqi; the Standard Sports Equipment Company, Chen Yuze; the Chinese Leprosy Relief Association, Gao Mingqiang; the Puyi Society, Chen Hanming; the Chinese Health Education Association, Xu Yi; the Huisheng Midwifery School, Xu Naiwu; the YMCA, Ling Xitao, and over twenty others. Wu Liguo presided over the meeting, and Lu Bingqian served as the secretary. It was resolved that the organization of the association would be divided into two departments: General Affairs and Exhibits. The General Affairs Department would be further divided into three groups: Administration, Storage, and Publicity. The Exhibits Department would be divided into three groups: School, Society, and Reference. Each group would have one director. The exhibition venue was tentatively set at the Puyi Society, and the exhibition would be held for three consecutive days from June 1st to 3rd. The school exhibits would include various items from kindergartens and primary schools, such as central education, subject-based education, creations, curriculum materials, testing materials, self-made teaching aids, life guidance, and administrative affairs. Middle schools would exhibit administration, teaching materials, self-made teaching aids, student and teacher work, creations, sports equipment, and models. The society exhibits would be divided into categories such as anti-drug, venereal disease, infectious disease, and family. The reference exhibits would be divided into categories such as books, instruments, models, and films. Society and reference exhibits would not be subject to review, while school exhibits would be reviewed. Furthermore, to expand publicity, the association planned to hold health lectures and performances and conduct essay competitions during the exhibition.

Scout Expert Mr. Gu Zhenglai's Remains to be Buried Today

Scout expert and former President of the Chinese Physical Education School, Mr. Gu Zhenglai, was admired for his learning and moral character. He dedicated his life to the country, committing himself to the Scout movement for the army, navy, and air force, supporting the revolution, and managing charitable affairs. His heroic achievements throughout his life are too numerous to mention. During this time of national crisis, when talent is urgently needed, unfortunately, Mr. Gu personally supervised the South City Defense Corps during the January 28th Incident last year, defending the local area, working tirelessly day and night. This led to overwork and illness. Despite treatment from both Chinese and Western medicine, the remedies proved ineffective, and he passed away at his Shanghai residence on July 7th of last year. Friends and relatives, close and distant, were deeply saddened by the news. Mr. Gu's lifelong friends, including Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Kaixian, Zhang Boling, Li Qifan, Ye Caizhen, Feng Liming, Huang Renzhi, and Shen Xinqing, are handling his funeral arrangements. It has been decided that today at 2:30 PM, a burial ceremony will be held for Mr. Gu's remains at the Christian cemetery in Song Park, Zhabei. Reverend Li from Moore Memorial Church will preside over the service, following Mr. Gu's wishes for a simple funeral. Trainees from the board of directors' Scout instructor training course and classmates will respectfully carry the coffin, moving from Yongxi Hall, turning from Taixielu Road onto Zhongshan Road, and proceeding to the Baptist Moore Memorial Garden on Song Park Road in Zhabei. It is also reported that senior officials and teams from the South City Defense Corps will participate. Mr. Gu had friends all over the country, and it is expected that many will participate in carrying the coffin, expressing their condolences.

Shooting Competition, Group A

Zhang Yingda Achieves Great Luck

Defeats Veteran Shen Lince in Final Shot

Result: 1000 Points to 986

Benal Ill, No Competition Today

Zhang Yingda enjoyed great luck in his final shot, defeating veteran Shen Lince to advance to the semi-finals in the Shanghai Amateur Group A shooting competition. He will soon compete against shooting champion Li Gongying. The match between the two was extremely slow, with each round lasting over three hours. The situation was dull until the later rounds, when it became tense. Shen had the advantage in the first round, leading with 500 points to 398. However, in the second round, Zhang shot smoothly. Even at the twentieth shot, Zhang was still 100 points behind (585 to 685). He then rallied, scoring 36, 44, 14, 5, and 12 in the next five shots, pulling ahead with 695 to 692. From then on, both sides scored high, averaging similar scores, with Shen regaining the lead shortly after. However, the difference was minimal. Nearing the end, Shen was still leading with 986 to 975. Unexpectedly, Zhang scored 25 points on his final shot, securing the final victory with 1000 points to 986. Shen can be said to have been extremely unlucky. British veteran Benal is ill, and his match today against Medina has been cancelled.
